O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	Oh, you, very wise sons, I have completed this book that is the end of the science of medicine and its fulfillment, and I have finished it by his explanations and by his declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to me in a vision that I should complete it with this treatise, which is part of the work of hands, that is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is fortified in our region and is drawn from all things, it has perished and been lost, and nothing remains of it except the small descriptions in books of the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and the foolishness, and the minds are closed and the knowledge is distant.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation;	It seems to me that I can revive it together with the order of this treatment according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation;
et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	and I will bring together the forms of cauterizing irons and other tools of the work with the explanation and preparation of it, as it is necessary.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	Because for the reason that no good masters of hands are found in our time, the art of medicine is extended.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who undertakes this to surpass in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, until he knows the judgment of the bones, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of all, and has knowledge of the bones and nerves and tendons and the number of joints, and the movement and resting of them, and the origin of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc;	Because, as Hippocrates says, "not to do something is bad, and with the work it is little.
et meismement en l’art de main.	And even in the art of handiwork.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes;	We tell you at the beginning of this book that those who are not familiar with the things mentioned before, if they attempt to do so, may go astray and harm people;
ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	such that I have often wanted many times more of those who deal with this science and if they abandon themselves to their own knowledge and experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col;	For I saw a foolish man who lanced an abscess of scrofula or boil from a woman's breast, and lanced the arteries from the boil;
por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	because so much blood issued out that the woman died in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans;	And I saw another foolish man who treated a stone from a man's gallbladder, and the stone was large;
si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	and took along with it a piece of the bladder, and died within three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I had already been called for the extraction, and saw the misalignment of the limb and the size of the stone, and if they cut it, it would die.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie;	And another miracle that took place in our care, of the duke of our land who had his leg broken, and with the breaking had a wound.
et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine;	And the miracle of ignorance kept the break over the wound with splints for a long time, and did not leave the wound without salt, and thus it ended.
et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie;	and the command that he not remove it quickly;
et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	and thus it remained until the leg was completely healed and the foot and came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe;	I was called to come to him, and hurried to remove the leg;
et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	And when I felt it dislocated, it was in pain and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner;	But all the ways of the corruption were already confirmed or the member, and could not be healed;
et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	and the corruption did not stop moving through the member until the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And I saw another method that crushed the abscess and became putrid, and then it inflamed due to its evil nature.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For putridity, when it is free of melancholic humor, does not need much if one only touches it with iron if it is in a place where everything can be completely removed that is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions:	And therefore, very dear son, you must know that the work of hands is divided into two divisions:
c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions;	that is to say, where it has been exposed to many positions;
et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	and I will show in each of these books where it has fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos.	Because of this, you should keep it a secret so that the foolish people cannot harm you.
Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez;	If you take your arms in a firm and steady manner, and use the best method so that by the grace of God you come to safety and are healthy.
et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit;	And leave the spreading diseases of poor health;
et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	And take your arms from what makes you doubt, and be in yourself so that you can come from this world to the other of glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens:	Galenus says in some of his admonitions:
«Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	«Do not take on the care of sick people who are not fools.»
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have devised this treatment in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez;	The first chapters are of fire cauteries and de-cauteries of medical water, and the chapters are ordered from the head to the feet.
et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	And the forms of instruments, and the irons of cauteries, and of everything that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses;	The second chapters are of cutting and piercing, and of wounds, and of arrow extractions, and similar things.
et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	And the chapters are ordered and the forms of instruments.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses;	The third chapters are of resetting dislocations and twists, and similar things.
et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	and is ordered to place the upper limbs in their proper places, and to shape the instruments.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	As we remember the work, it is necessary that I tell the quality of the aid and the harm of each ingredient.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus;	The quality of aid, and its harm, is the longest and most subtle of speech and secret sciences;
et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu;	and many wise men spoke about it, and agreed on this.
et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	and I do not know much about it, because I lack the length.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions:	I say that cauterization helps universally in all matters where there is matter, whether the matter:
c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	is to know whether it is hot and with matter, or dry and without matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide;	In a hot and dry environment, they assembled together and said that fire cauterization is a great help.
et li autre dirent le contraire:	And the others said the opposite:
que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	that fire cauterization does not help diseases that come from heat and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour;	Because the nature of fire is hot, and should not be cured by heat, nor by dryness;
et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	and those who said the opposite claimed that fire cauterization helps greatly with hot and dry diseases that come from within men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you compare the body of the person and its moisture to the hot fire, you heat the body.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this saying.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have found it once by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens;	And in any case, no one interferes with it except those who have experienced it, and know from long use the chapter of cauterizations, and the diversity of men's complexions, and their dispositions and causes of diseases, and the symptoms and time of healing;
des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	of other constitutions we have no fear at all, even in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And all the patients gathered and agreed to the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	And know, my sons, that cauterization with fire is one of the secrets of cures, and of greater benefit than cauterization with hot medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fever is simple, and comes only to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members unless it is named.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation;	The burning remedies come from one member to another by moving away, and bring diseases of great relief to the affected limb.
et par aventure ocit lou malaide.	and perhaps it is the pain.
Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The fever for its height and because of the goodness of its substance does not cause harm, if there is no excess.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses;	And I have found that you would find by experiment and by the length of service and study that I have put into the art, and it was above the truth of things;
et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant;	And because I apologize for the length of the language, as it does not please me only that I give you the secret that is hidden or fire, and the quality of the work, how it cures diseases of the body, as the philosopher says in demonstrating;
or le recevez en vos pensees.	or receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	And know, child, that they should be done with cauterizations in what manner they should be made, and they will ask for them.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere;	And I say that cauterization is beneficial in all cases, because the harmful substances are removed by the help of cauterization;
et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	and indeed it is even necessary for pain that cannot wait until the time when the greatest harm comes to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire;	And never think, dear child, as the foolish ones do;
car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue;	for the disease that is healed by cauterization has no return;
et il le dient ensi;	and it is said thusly;
mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	but it is not as they think, for cauterization is but medicine that moves the humors, and dries up the humors that are the cause of the pain, and is more effective than any other medicine due to its swiftness of action and the virtue of its work and its authority.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut;	And it is possible that the disease comes only according to the humor and the constitution of the patient and its power;
et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie;	and are assembled in it the superfluities by the acquisition of meats and similar things, if not cauteries administered to him where he has little superfluity and moisture, as cauteries for dense pain, and similar things, and the pain does not return.
mais ce avient poc.	but this happened little.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir;	And many people do not understand why cauteries are called the tail of medicine, and this is to see;
mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	but they do not believe little that cauteries are of value after medicine, but rather their understanding is false, and cauteries are the tail of medicine because when we administer methods of cures in any disease and they do not work, then we administer the cautery, and it is valuable.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is important to understand that cauterization is a part of medical treatment, not according to the intention of those who are misled.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance;	The old ones said that the cautery of an instrument of gold is more effective than iron, and they did not say what else but for the quality of gold and the expensiveness of its substance.
et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes;	And they said that the heads of the cautery do not make pain, but it is not to see because I have experienced it, and I have found that it is to see in some people.
et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	And the cautery of gold is more effective than iron, as they said.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez;	And whenever you heat an instrument of gold, you should not be afraid when it is hot because of the color of gold, and it has already cooled.
et s’on le chaufe trop;	and if they are heated too much;
si font au feu;	if they are done by fire;
et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	and then they have enough restraint.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And therefore we use the fire cauterization that we have prepared for our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or I have ordered this chapter on the shoulder joints from the feet, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	The fire cauterization oil.
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is valuable against moisture and cold on the head, and it is done for two reasons: because of a disease called "soda", and because of many humors that descend from the joint to the ears, and due to many dreams and tooth pain and throat pain, and indeed for all diseases that come from cold as paralysis and soda and apoplexy and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir;	The form of this cautery is that the hairs are removed by medical means, changing the shape of the head three or four times, according to the virtues and the age and the custom of the hair, which the patient can bear.
et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	and then make the hair of the patient again.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis;	And then let him sit crossed between your hands, and put his hands on top of yours;
aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz;	after put the root of your palm above the root of his nose between his two eyes;
et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	When you come to me with your two fingers, if they bleed profusely, heat the cauterizing iron called "olivare", of which this is the shape:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant;	And place it on the joint, which is marked with ink, and move it back and forth gently in twisting your hand little by little;
puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit;	Then slowly remove your hand, and reward the joint if you see the bone slightly;
et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit;	And if you do not see it, then continue with the cauterizing iron until you see the bone as I have told you.
aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors;	Then take a little thread, and wrap it softly in cotton, and place it on the joint, and leave it for three hours.
aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre;	after put this cotton in butter;
et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	and leave it on until the wound is healed;
aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	after treat the wound with the ointment called "tetra-pharmacon" until it is healed.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge;	And the ancients said that the longer the wound remains open, the more it purges;
et por ce si aide mues.	and for this reason, it helps to heal.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these said that one should burn the cauterizer until a part of the bone is charred, and then remove what has been charred from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors;	And the other says that one should apply the cauterizing iron as gently as possible above, and push it as hard as one can to remove bone as wide as a needle that women put in their hair for the reason that the humors come out easily;
et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte;	and one should leave the wound open for a long time;
aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	after that, one should cure and dress it.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor;	And these two methods of cauterization do not seem to be good in all cases, except in some men where there is a way of fear;
et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier;	and it seems to me that I should leave it.
car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres;	because the joints are weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we testify in other members;
et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	and even when the joint affected by pain is weak by nature, and the first appearance of cauterization is safer and more appropriate for me, and from this I work in the future accordingly.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	of the ancient pain of the main
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres;	When in general the head comes with chronic pain that lasts a long time, one should use ointments and pills called "cochie", and cleansing of the head and eyes and plasters.
et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	and if they do the fire cauterization that we have mentioned before, it does not help.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit;	Take care if the patient is of a strong constitution and is not too cold;
adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	then cauterize with that fire cauterization that we have mentioned above.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»;	After cauterization on each eyebrow to the bone, as we have mentioned before, and do the cauterization called "vasselz".
et est I leus en coi on met ventouses;	and is the place where suction cups are used;
et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os:	and lift your hand so you do not press too hard on the bone:
li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors;	the hairs cause greater pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will speak of it there.
et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	and it is necessary that the cauterizing irons for the horns be more delicate than the one with which one cauterizes the midline of the forehead, and this is the form:
dou cautere dou chief	for the fire cauterization
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie:	When in one part of the head sudden pain comes, and the disease is extended to the oil, and the patient is purged by medicines that are changed, and the other cures that I have said in the division of diseases are done, and all this does not help much:
adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	Therefore, if it is necessary to cauterize according to two methods, that is to say, by means of medicine or fire.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir;	The cauterization by medicine is such that you press a piece of alum, and remove the scab and reapply it with a small amount of the same thing, and then make the temple or place where the pain is located in a certain way so that you can replace the piece of alum outside the skin;
et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres;	and when it is replaced, if it holds and restrains well, leave it thus for twelve hours;
et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III;	then remove it and treat afterwards with the piece of garlic, and leave the wound thus for two or three days;
puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	Then place a hot poultice on top until the pain subsides.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the application of ointment until they are healed.
et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	And if you see that some burning remedies that I have written or prescribed are not working, then treat them with other burning remedies.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The fire cauterization is done in this way.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the cauterizing iron of such a shape:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance;	And it is called "closed" because the head is made in the shape of a clod or it has little burns, and in the middle has a small appearance.
et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse;	And it is placed on the painful limb, and hold your hand and gently stir the fire until half of the surface is burned.
et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	and gently touch your hand so the artery does not burn, which is nearby, and bleed abundantly of blood.
Aprés met coton en awe de seil, et met sor le leu par III jors;	After put cotton in a sling, and put it on the limb for three days;
puis i met coton moilliet em burre, et puis cure le leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	then put cotton moistened in butter, and then heal the limb of inflammation until it is healthy;
et se tu vuelz cauterize ceste emigraine avec le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare», a tout la pointe, et te garde de coper l’artere en ceste emigraine qui n’est mie anciaine.	and if you want to cauterize this wound with the cauterizing iron called "cultellare", at all the point, and keep from covering the artery in this wound which is not ancient.
de emigraine	of the wound
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans;	When you treat this wound as we have said in the division of diseases, and it does not improve, and you see that the cauterizing iron before says of medicine and hot iron does not hurt him a little, then it is necessary that you extinguish the cauterizing iron called "cultellare" until it is white;
et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os;	and if the bone is fractured with a line of half a finger's width, and you take your hand once, and hold the artery so that it does not come near the bone;
et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez;	and guard the jaw that moves when moved, and the nerves have no regard except for the moving ones and that spasm does not cause harm, and guard against the corruption of blood from the artery when it is cut, or cutting into it has great fear and immediately to those who do not know, and who are not studied and experienced;
et laisse l’uevre em mi voie;	and let the work be in moderation.
mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	but I will tell you how to stop the bleeding when the artery is cut, and I will show you where it appears in this book.
Et se tu vois que cist cauteres ne soffise mie a la maladie, et li malaides est soffrans, cauterize le enmi le chief ausi com nos avons dit, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And if you see that this cauterization is not enough for the disease, and the patient is suffering, cauterize it with fire as we have said, and treat the wound until it is healed.
et se tu vues, aministre le cautere que nos avons dit ou chapistre de l’estraction de l’artere, avec le cautere qui ait II coutelz;	And if you see that the cauterization is not enough, administer the cauterization that we have said or in the chapter of the extraction of the artery, with the cauterizer that has two blades.
et est cist cauteres millors de celui et plus aidans.	And this cauterization is better than the other and more helpful.
de la dolor des oreilles de part froidor	of the pain of the ears from cold
Quant en l’oreille vient dolor de froit, et on i a ovreit de medicines solutives et des autres cures que nos avons dit en la division, et li dolors ne se muet, adonques eschaufe cest cautere qui est apelez «poins», de coi ci est li forme:	When the ear hurts from cold, and medicines have been applied and other treatments that we have said in the division, and the pain does not move, then warm this cautery called "poins", of which is the form:
Aprés pointoie tout entor l’oreille malaide, ou entor les II se la dolor tient en ambedous, et t’esloigne un poc ensus de la racine de l’oreille puis que tu as signiet le leu d’enche;	After pricking all around the ear, wherever the pain is felt on both sides, and move it slightly away from the root of the ear, then you have correctly identified the earwax.
et ait X poins entor chescune oreille;	and apply X drops around each ear.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure the ear until it is healthy.
de la torture de la bouche	of the torture of the mouth
Torture qui doit estre curee par cautere nen est fuers que de celles que muevent de fleume, si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladie;	This torture should only be treated by cauterization is no more than those that move with the flux, as we have said in the division of diseases.
et ne faire point de cautere as semblances que vienent de sechor et de spame de ners.	and do not use cauterization with similar substances that come from sechors and spit of men.
Quant tu cures ceste semblance de torture qui muet de fleume d’ydres et d’espurgemens de chief et de gargarisme, et ceu ne vaut, adonc covient que tu cauterizes le malaide de III cauteres:	When you treat this resemblance of torture that moves from the stream of waters and of purging of the head and of gargling, and it does not help, then it is necessary that you cauterize the pain with three cauteries:
l’une en la racine de l’oreille, et l’autre un poc defuers la temple, et le tier en l’ajostement des II levres;	one at the root of the ear, and the other a little later the temple, and the third in the position of the two lips;
et met le cautere en la partie qui apert saine, et li fai cautere endroit le chief de l’oreille desus un poc desoz la corne dou chief, et un autre en la temple ausi longe com uns poce;	and put the cauteries in the part that opens healthy, and do the cauterization at the top of the ear above a little out of the horn of the head, and another in the temple as long as one finger;
et laisse le cautere tant sus que li moitiez dou keur soit arse;	and leave the fire cautery as long as half of the wound is healed.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	This is the shape of the fire cautery.
Et est li semblance dou cutellaire que nos avons mise devant, mais il est un poc plus subtilz et covient que li coutelz soit un poc plus gros;	And this is the shape of the cauterizing iron that we have placed before, but it is a bit more delicate and it is necessary that the knife be a bit larger.
aprés cure lou leu si com j’ai devant dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After curing the limb as I have said before, until it is healed.
Quant apoplexie est ancieinne et tu la cures ensi com nos avons dit, et il ne profite mie, et li malaides n’ait fievre, adonques li fai IIII cauteres:	When apoplexy is old and you treat it as we have said, and it does not improve, and the pains do not have fever, then make four cauterizations:
II sus les II cornes dou chief, et I emmi le chief, et I ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz» si com nos avons devant dit, et lou derrien cautere sus la bouche de l’estomac;	Above the two upper horns of the shoulder, and below the chief, and also the one that is called "vasselz" as we have previously said, and behind the fire above the mouth of the stomach;
et soit curez si com nos avons dit devant.	and treat it as we have said before.
de litargie	For laziness
A cest maladie covient doner au malaide yeres grans et pilules mondifians le cerveil;	For this disease, one should give the patient large and modified brain-shaped pills;
aprés reis lou chief dou malaide tout, et li met sus l’occipite l’emplaustre de sinapi qui est escrit ou traitier des emplastres;	after rubbing the entire shoulder of the patient with the mustard plaster written or used to treat ointments;
et c’est li maniere dou cautere:	and this is the way of the fire cauterization:
si lou fai si com j’ai dit.	as I have said.
S’il est sanez ensi, boin est;	If he is thus healthy, good.
et s’il ne l’est, se li fai III cauteres des emmi le chief en dessendant jusc’a col, et ait d’espaice entre chescun cautere I doi de gros;	And if he is not, do three fire cauterizations on the neck from above down to the collarbone, and leave space between each cauterization of one large span.
et le cure si com les autres, et se tu i vues ajoster, et li malaides est soffrans, se li fai I cautere en mileu;	And the treatment is as for the others, and if you have seen it stuck, and the pain is great, do one cauterization in the middle.

de la froidor dou chief	of the cold of the head
Il covient que li chief soit mundifiez de yeres et de ceu que nos avons devant dit;	It is necessary that the head be cleaned of years and of what we have previously said.
aprés reis le chief dou malaide, puis li fai cautere emmi le chief et sus chescune corne, et I derrier et III sus l’espinee dou col;	After cleaning the head of the hairs, then perform a fire cauterization on the head and each horn, and behind and three times above the spine of the neck.
et se tu en as plus mestier, et li cors est moiste et li malaides est soffrans, et li maladie est fors, se li fai IIII cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos;	And if you have more trouble, and the body is wet and the hairs are in pain, and the disease is far, then perform four cauterizations above the spine of the back.

de l’epilempsie	of epilepsy
Li epilentiques ne doit useir de cautere fuers que cil qui est fleumatique, et covient premier mondifier le cerveil de yeres et d’autres cures que nos avons dites en la division quant li malaides est grans et soffrans de penre medicine.	Those who suffer from epilepsy should not use cauterization except for that which is fleshy, and it is first necessary to modify the brain of years and other treatments that we have mentioned in the division when the pains are large and severe with pain medicine.
Et se c’est uns enfes qui ne lou puisse soffrir, se li fai gargarisme et mastication mondifiant le cerveil sovent avec bones viandes;	And if it is a child who cannot bear it, make him gargle and chew, modifying the brain often with good meat.
aprés li reis lou chief em mileu, et i fai I cautere selonc ce que nos avons dit devant, et I cautere sus lou vassel, et sus chescune corne;	After the child's head is in the middle, and do cauterization according to what we have said before, and cauterize above the vein, and above each horn.
et se li malaides est fors et soffrans, se li fai cauteres si com j’ai dit a celui qui ait paralisie et mollification de cors, sus l’espinee dou dos et dou col, et soit li cauteres olivier selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	And if the pain is outside and severe, do cauterization as I said to those who have paralysis and softening of the neck, above the spine of the back and neck, and let the cauterization be with olive oil according to the way I said.
Se li malaides est enfes, se li fai I cautere subtil selonc ceste maniere:	If the pain is intense, then perform the following delicate cauterization method:
Quant par la cause de melancolie sunt les superfluitez ou les moistors corrumpues et fleume grosse, adonques lou cauterize de teils cauteres com nos avons dit a celui qui ait paralisie.	When due to melancholy, the excess or corrupted moisture and fluid is large, then use the following cautery made of parts as we have said for those who have paralysis.
Et se par la cause de melancolie est li superfluitez declinans a melancolie, et est li cors dou malaide moistes, adonc li done a boivre chose par coi li cervelz soit mundifiez, selonc ceu qu’il est devant en la division.	And if due to melancholy, the excess or corrupted moisture is declining towards melancholy, and the course of the bad pain is wet, then give it to drink something by which the brain is cleansed, according to what it is before in the division.
Aprés reis lou chief dou malaide;	After removing the cause of the pain;
aprés fai I torteil de lin bien fait, ausi com I cercle, si le met emmi le chief;	after making a well-made bandage, like a circle, and placing it on the head;
et li malaides sié croisiez, et soit bien tenus de toutes pars;	and the pains are crossed, and held tightly from all sides;
aprés presente le linement, et vaut mues de burre de berbis ancien;	after applying the liniment, and it is good to use old bearberry ointment;
et lou chaufe a feu tempreement, si que li dois s’on li boute le puisse soffrir;	and the heat of the fire is tempered, so that he can bear it if possible;
aprés vuide le cercle par dedens emmi le chief, et lou laisse refroidier;	after emptying the circle from inside and placing it on the head, and letting it cool;
et fai ce a malaide chescune semaine une fois avec autre governement boin, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and do this to the pain every week once with good management until they are healed.
Ou se tu vues cauterize lou en faisant poins plusors a tot le cautere.	Where you have seen cauterization with making points all over the cauterizer.
Ceste maniere de cautere amoistit le cerveil igaument;	This method of cauterization moistens the brain excessively.
et puis met sus coton moilliet en burre et en graisse de geline.	Then place a moistened cotton ball in butter and goose fat.
de l’awe des eulz	of the eyes'
Quant awe vient premierement as eulz par les signes que j’ai dit en la division, adonques encomence et done boivre au malaide chose mundifiant le chief, et le warde de toutes moistors, et lou fai suer ou bain plusors fois a jeun.	When the eye comes firstly to the eyes by the signs that I have said in the division, then begin and give to the patient a remedy mundifying the head, and keep it from all moisture, and make it sweat or bathe it several times at fasting.
Aprés li comande a rere son chief, et li fai cautere emmi le chief, et li fai II cauteres sus les II temples se li dessendemens de l’awe est as II eulz ensamble, ou en I se li dessendemens est en I;	After that, instruct the patient to turn his head, and apply the cauterization on his head, and perform two cauterizations on both temples simultaneously, or if one eye is not present, then one.
et cope a tout le cautere toutes les voines et les arteres que sont desoz le keur, et soient li cautere lonc selon lou large de la temple;	And cover all the cauterization with veins and arteries that are outside the cranium, and let the cauterization be long according to the width of the temple.
et te warde de decorrement de sanc, et se tu vois trop de sanc issir, si li estainche de teil pooir com tu as.	And watch for bleeding from the wounds, and if you see too much blood flowing, use a towel or cloth as needed.
Et je t’enseignerai en l’estraction des arteres et a l’incision la cautele coment tu l’estencheras;	And I will teach you in the extraction of arteries and in the incision, how you will perform it.
et aucune fois fait on cautere ou hatereil desoz les II os derrier.	Never perform cauterization or heating on the two lower bones.
dou cors des larmes	The path of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont ancienes et acostumees et sont sus les voines, ou delez les arteres que sont en l’aparance dou chief defors;	When the tears of the eyes are old and accustomed and are above the veins, or over the arteries that are in the appearance of the main difference.
et on voit que c’est des superfluitez froides fleumatiques, adonques li fai le cautere que j’ai dit en l’encomencement de l’awe dessendant as eulz:	And we see that it is a superfluous cold, flabby flesh, therefore the cauterization that I mentioned at the beginning of this chapter, descend upon them.
I cautere emmi le chief, et II cauteres sus les II temples, et II cauteres ou haiterel desoz les II os;	I cauterize the main, and two cauterize above the two temples, and two cauterize or heating outside the two bones.
et s’il i a besoigne plus, si le cauterize saigement desus le sorcil a tout I petit cautere.	If there is more, then cauterize carefully above the shoulder with a small firebrand.
dou cors des larmes par dedens les eulz	through the courts of tears by through the eyes
Quant tu le medicines selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et il ne profite mie, adonques done a boivre a malaide III nuis cochies;	When you apply the remedies according to what we have said in the chapter, and it does not help, then give him three drinks with bad taste.
aprés li reis le chief, et li fai cautere ou mileu dou cautere olivaire;	After the king's head, and the face, and the cauterization or middle of the cauterization with oil.

et te warde de l’artere que tu ne la coper.	And watch out for the artery that you do not cover.
Et c’est li forme dou cautere qui est apelez «clavilis»:	And this is the form of the cauterization called "clavilis":
Quant li papiere de l’oil est mollifie de maladie et de moistor, adonques la cautarize de cest cautere qui est apelez «olivare».	When the paper of the oil is softened by disease and moisture, then cauterize with this cauterization called "olivare".
de coi ci est li forme:	For this reason, this is the shape:
Et se tu vues si fai II cauteres sus les II sorcis ausi lons com li sorcilz sont;	And if you see that this is done, make two cauterizations above the two spikes as long as the spikes are;
et n’i lassiez mie la main fors que tant que li tierce partie de la papiere soit arse, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit.	and do not leave the hand except until the third part of the paper is burned, according to the manner that I have said.
dou poil qui point l’oil	the hairs that do not point the oil
Aucune fois avient que li poil des oilz sont convertit au pardedens, et poignent l’oil, et i fait on cauteres selonc II manieres:	Never have it so that the hairs of the eyes are converted to pardons, and they hold the eye, and then make one cautery in two ways:
c’est a savoir de feu, ou de medicine ardant.	that is to say, by fire, or by burning medicine.
Ou cautere de feu comande au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient lons et igals;	Or the fire cauterization commands the patient to let the hairs grow long and even;
et s’il le poignent a lor nassance, se li estraint les eulz qu’il ne se muevent tant qu’il naissent.	And if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il naissent et i sont igalz, adonques met le malaide en ton sain;	When they are born and are even, then put the misaligned part in its proper place;
aprés seigne sus la papiere des eulz une figure que soit ausi com li fuelle dou mirte, et soit li comencemens dou signe delez les poilz;	After, above the paper of the eyes, there is a figure that should be as such as the one of the mirror, and it should be the beginning of the sign among the hairs;
puis i met coton moilliet en glaire d’uef et muscillaige de persillion sus l’oil, puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then put soft cotton moistened in egg yolk and mint oil on the eye, then heat the cauterizing iron of which this is the form:
Aprés cauterize sus la figure que tu as signiet poc et poc mout de fois, que li keurs soit ars lai endroit;	Then cauterize slowly and gently many times, until the healer is at the right place;
et li signes de la santeit de l’uevre est que tu voies la papiere retraite, et les poilz levez a la pointure de l’oil;	and the signs of the health of the work is that you see the paper retreating, and the hairs raised to the height of the oil.
adonques lieve ta main, et laisse ensi III jors, puis i met coton moilliet en burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	then lightly touch your hand, and leave it thus for three days, then put cotton moistened in butter on the burn until the scar is formed.
aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
Et se aprés ceu vienent li poilz, et li papiere est mollifie adonques rencomence le cautere sus cel leu meisme, si com tu as fait premiers;	and if after this the hairs come back, and the paper is softened, then restart the cauterization on the same place, as you did first.
et se li poil sont defuer, si le cauterize tant que li papiere soit levee a son leu natureil, et soit igals, et ne poignent mie li poil l’oil.	and if the hairs are lacking, then cauterize until the paper is raised to its natural height, and is even, and does not prick at the base of the oil.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il laisse les poilz tant qu’il soient grans et igalz, puis fai de parchemin la forme de la foille de mirte;	The cauterizing iron of medicine is that you command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even, then make a piece of parchment in the shape of a leaf of myrtle.
puis pren de savon fransois et de vive chalz, de chescun une .З., et broie ensamble bien;	Then take French soap and live chalk, one of each, and grind them together well.
et le fai hastanment, si qu’il ne refroide, puis en espant sus la forme que tu es fait sicom la foille dou mirte, et met sus la papiere des eulz;	And make it into a paste, so that it does not cool, then spread it over the shape you have made like a leaf of myrtle, and put it on the paper of the eyes.
et se li maladie tient en I oil soulement, si doit on ovrer en I, et se en ambedous ausi;	And if the patient holds the evil in only one eye, then you should cover it with a bandage, and do the same for the other.
et met desoz l’oil coton moilliet en abin d’uef;	and place a soft cotton cloth under the elbow.
et li chiés dou malaide soit en ton sain et met ton doi mostrant sus la medicine, et presse I poc et lou muef toutes les fois que li malaide sent mordication de la medicine, car il sent mordication ausi com de feu.	and the patient with the pain should be in a healthy position and place the hand above the medicine, and press and move it gently every time the pain feels burning from the medicine, for it feels burning like fire.
Quant tu as ceu fait longement, si oste la medicine a ton doit.	When you have done this for a long time, then take the medicine to your mouth.
Et quant li mordication sera passee, si leve le leu d’awe, et rewarde se tu vois la papiere levee ausi com s’ele estoit levee par constraignement de feu ou par incision;	And when the burning pain has passed, lift the limb from the fire, and reward if you see the paper raised as it was raised by constraint of fire or by incision.
et s’il est ensi, si est bien.	and if so, then it is well.
Se ceu non, si remet encor de la medicine sus lou leu ou li medicine n’ait ovreit, tant que tes ovraiges soit igalz, et tes eulz mis a point;	If not, then put the medicine back on the limb or the medicine has not worked, until your actions are equal and your eyes are focused.
puis met sus coton moilliet en burre tant que li keurs ars soit cheus, aprés cure le leu de l’oignement qui est apelez «dyafenis» et d’autre, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place a moistened cotton swab on the affected area until the pus is removed, then treat the wound with the ointment called "diaphanis" and other, until it is healed.
Et se t’est mestier que tu te warde bien a ton ovraige par grant warde qu’il ne chiece point de la medicine as eulz.	And if you have the task to stay within your work, do so with great care, lest you not cut into the wrong parts of the medicine.
Et se li papiere devient mole aprés, et li poil poignent en l’oil, si recomence la medicine sus celui leu qui est mollifiez de la papiere proprement, ensi com tu as fait devant;	And if the paper becomes thin afterwards, and the hairs are pricked in the oil, then restart the treatment on the softened area of the paper properly, as you have done before.
aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	After the treatment until it is healed.
et c’est li forme de la fuelle dou mirte:	And this is the form of the foot of the mouse:
Et saichés que li eul des homes sont divers en grandor et en petitece, et selonc ceu soit tes constraignemens;	And it is known that the eyes of men are different in size and smallness, and according to what you are constrained by.
et ne soit mie reponue li droite voie a celui cui est li estude de cest art.	and is not immediately returned to the proper way to the one who has studied this art.
de la cure de fistule par cautere	of the treatment of a fistula by fire cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere.	When you treat a fistula as we have described in the division of diseases, and your treatments are not effective, then it is necessary to cauterize it in this manner.
Comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain;	instruct the patient to put his head on your shoulder.
et teigne li menistres son chief entre tes mains en teil maniere qu’il ne se mueve, ne ne demoinne son chief;	and clean the wound around his head between your hands in such a way that it does not move and does not dislodge his head.
aprés met coton moilliet en abin d’uef ou en jus de persillion sus l’oil;	after put moistened cotton on the wound or in juice of parsley over the oil.
aprés chaufe le cautere qui est teilz:	after heat the cauterizing iron that is ready.
et est chevez au chief si com li forme d’une penne de vouteul, ensamble la queil soit li cautere;	and it is shaped like a pen of vulture, together with the quill so that it is the cauterizing iron.
se tu vues, si soit apointé des l’un chief dusc’a l’autre, et se tu vues, si soit ausi com une tente;	if you see that one is appointed to the other, and if you see that it is as if a tent;
mais toutevoie, cist qui est chevez vaut mues por ton ovraige.	but always, this that is sewn is better for your work.
Aprés presse la fistule s’ele est overte, et en trai la porriture, et la seche;	After pressing the fistula if it is open, and in taking the pus, and drying;
et s’ele est close, si la oevre, et trai fuers la bowe;	and if it is closed, then open, and take out the pus;
aprés met sus le cautere chaut forment, et tien ta main au cautere a la partie dou neif ensus de l’oil, que ta mains ne faice folie;	after put the fire cautery very hot, and hold your hand on the cautery to the part of the knee above the oil, that your hand does not do foolishness;
et met le cautere en la graisse de l’oil, et la corromp.	and put the fire cautery in the grease of the oil, and corrupt.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cauterizing iron at the bone, that would be good.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors;	If not, if you must restart the cauterization again, and if you have the skill, leave it for three days;
aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers;	then put cotton moistened in butter on it, and apply the ointment of the desiccating cure until it is healed, and if forty days have passed and it is not healed, then put on corrosive medicine until the bone is exposed;
et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	and the rest according to what it would come in its chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a certain method of cauterizing a fistula that no one of the ancients mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu;	For a fistula, and feel the limb;
aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	then put in the wound the subtle camomile of which this is the form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc;	and they do with the quantity of a certain amount of mud;
et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil;	and hold your hand or grip firmly, and the hairs do not move, until the mud sets and does not flow to its oil;
et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe:	and it is necessary to put above the oil on the hair a soft cotton pad in front of or behind:
li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	the mud if the limb of the fistula, and the healthy through marvelous healing.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	And if the fistula is healed by the cauterization that we have mentioned, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then it is necessary to administer purgatives to the nose, and to bring the fistula back to its proper place in the nostril as it should be.
des crevaices en levres	cracked lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times there are cracks in the lips that are called "hair", and at the same time in the lips of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks as we have mentioned in the divisions, and the treatment does not help, then heat a small cauterizing iron in this form:

aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	after healing the limb of the cerate until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the groin
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule;	When an abscess occurs at the root of the tongue or in the bladder, or in the palate, or at the roots of the teeth, after it has become putrid and runs and becomes swollen and becomes a fistula;
et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie:	and you cure it as we have said in the sections, and it does not improve.
adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule;	Therefore, it is necessary that you have the cauterization according to the size of the fistula;
aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu;	after the puncture or opening of the fistula, and keep your hand until the iron goes to the bottom of the wound and behind the bone;
et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do so once or twice, after curing what we have said in the cures, until it is healed.
et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin;	and if they are treated thusly, it is good;

dou movement des dens	movement of the teeth
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain;	When the teeth are softened by moisture and the roots move, and you treat it with medicine but it does not work, then put the head of the pain in your mouth.
aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent;	After heating the cauterizer of which the form will come later in some manner, you put a sponge on the tooth.
et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent;	and insert the cauterizer deeply, and hold your hand so that the pain feels the heat coming to the root of the tooth.
aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit;	After lightly touching your hand and begin the cauterization according to your will;
aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	Then fill the hairs of their mouth with salt water, and let them drink for an hour and then rest.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in this way, the tooth that was moving is confirmed, and the softened gums are held back, and the moisture is corrupted and dried up.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres:	When pain from a tooth comes from cold, or if there is cold or swelling, and the medical treatments do not work, then it is necessary to cauterize in two ways:
et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	and cauterization with butter and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain;	Cauterization with butter is such that you take butter from a fresh cow, and the end in an iron or brass spoon;
aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez;	After taking cotton and wrapping it around the tip of a tent peg, and wetting it with warm water, and placing it on the painful tooth firmly and holding it until it is cooled;
et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	and then do it often enough until its effect reaches the root of the tooth, and if you see that wetting the cotton and flax in warm water, and placing it on the aching tooth, and placing hot iron on it until the effect reaches the movement of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide;	The fire cauteries are such that you can grasp a piece of iron or brass, and it should be large enough that the effect does not reach the mouth of the wound.
aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez;	After heating the cautery, from which the form will come after, and place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cauterizing is cooled.
fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	Do this often, because the pain will be as strong the same day or the next.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer;	And it is necessary that the pain fill its mouth with good butter in the urgency of this cauterizing, and then apply it.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	This is the shape of the cauterizing tool:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir;	And make the cauterizing as you wish, and according to what you have.
et c’est li forme de la caine:	This is the shape of the cauterizing tool:
des scrophules	of hydroceles
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie;	When the scrofulous glands are swollen and cold, and do not obey digestion by medicines, then heat the hair burning cautery after this, and have two openings for the fumes to issue out of the other side;

Li forme de la cainne:	The shape of the jaw:

de la toust	of the whole

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains. dou cautere de pleuresin	fire cauterization

de ydropisie	de l’estomac
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not useful for hydropsy, except in the manner called "ascletyes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods that we have said in divisions, and your treatment does not help, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the wound, and one above the stomach, and one above the liver, and one above the spleen, and one behind the back above the spine, and one at the worst place;
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cautery be close to the edge of the wound.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	After leaving the cautery in place for a while to cauterize, do not let go of the care for the wound after the cautery.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing will proceed quickly, and both intentions will be accomplished with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cautery for the belly should be like the one we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that for the back should be oval-shaped, as it is shown before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen to the one who is hydroptic, and are plain of a yellowish color, it is necessary that you cauterize above the back between the auricular and the annular.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lightly touch the skin with the cauterizing iron, moving towards the direction of return.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus avoiding the yellowish parts, and let the cauteries be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After making two incisions on each leg at the tip of the needle-like instrument;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And either cauterize the long one behind the knee and the other in front of it, within the leg;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations over a longer period to cure what is inside.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After the cure of the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the bandage
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When the solution of the belly comes from cold and moisture, as long as the retentive and digestive virtues that are in the stomach and in the intestines are blocked, and cannot be cured by any means of treatments;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the painful and very skilled patient, if you make great cauterization above the stomach according to what he has spoken before or stomach cauterization, in cauterization circulates.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and IV cauterizations around the abdomen subtly to all the delicate cauterization fork, and II cauterizations above the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the abundance of moisture and the patient suffering from pain, then apply cauterization above the knuckle, and cauterization on each joint, and two small cauterizations below the stomach, for the cure is beneficial when it has good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of worms
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the emorrhoids are at their foundation, or one or more, and are ancient and are large humors cold and moist corrupted, and are cured as we have said in divisions, and it does not improve, if you make cauterizations:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Above the spine of the back, which is all before unaccustomedly little by little in triangulating, and with a cauterizing iron of two degrees.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the meat does not cook, and one sees the face swell, then the face is burned with a large cauterizing iron across the stomach, as it is previously described, and the other above the liver, and the other across the entire cauterizing iron.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	And leave the cauterizing iron long and tense.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, the limb as long as it is healthy.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the cartilage which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut the hair, if it scorches the cauterizing iron which seems like a razor, then put it all burned on top of the hair that is being cut.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand remain until the fire cauterizes the vein at its birth, from which the bleeding stops.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this once or twice, and if there is much blood, cauterize each as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of wounds until they are healed.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large fire brand, it will have greater help.
de plaie mal curee	of a poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the wound cannot be suffered by a surgeon or opened, as we will tell in its place, then a bad disease comes that cannot be healed except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any comes with a fistula, and it is inflamed and discharged putrid and corrupted moisture, then you must provide for the whole of a thin tent, and guard that you cleanse the tent as much as possible.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After sharpening the fire brand like a razor, and inserting it into the fistula according to the amount that enters, and then restart the cauterization until the wound is cleansed and healed, once, or twice, or three times, according to the amount of need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and watch for the vein that is cut, and large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the center of the bladder and intestine, then watch for these areas, and do not perform any other procedures except in the area where it is needed, and think that it is not healed.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after healing the area as long as it is healthy, and if there are any wounds, remove them, and the matter is removed along with the tension, then cleanse that the area is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matter is not removed, cleanse that the area is torn, and corrupt the bone at the source.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And thus, as one of those that we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold comes to the back, and with great heaviness, and does not take the form of a woman, then it is necessary that you do cauterization on both sides of the back with the clavile cautery that we have previously mentioned.
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	And if we cauterize it in the middle, it will have three cauterizations in a line, and they will be greater help.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and easily affected by cold and moisture, and the hairs retain urine, then do cauterization in the part in front of the bladder, where the hair begins to grow, and on both sides, and let each cauterization be as long as a needle.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and if you have a fever afterward, do the fire cautery on the back, or if you have a fever, do it.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the fire cautery be done in the form previously mentioned.
de la marris	of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the wound is cold and moist, and does not leave any room for healing, and the flowers are corrupted and their termination is late;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, they cause great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	therefore it is necessary to do the fire cautery around the wound, as we have said or the fire cautery of the bladder, and two fire cautery afterward on the back.
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the fire cautery be done as we have said.
de la hainche	of the waist
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the thick, viscous moisture descends to the hip of the back, and for this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together.
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found in the lower part of the hip, so it is necessary to cauterize the pain above the hip bone with a cautery similar to a circle, and sign before the bone as it turns, so that the hip is inside the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cautery is such as those used to cauterize the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if this cautery is not present, make three cauteries of large olive oil, and let the cautery be applied as all the others.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the care as long as they are healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the side of the hip, and it is from cold and moisture, and the hairs are curled as we have said in the division and the treatment does not help, and the disease is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	then it is necessary that you purge the hairs of the large humors from bad-smelling pills or other good-smelling pills similar.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you do the cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of the cauterization is as follows in two ways:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, together with hot medicines and fire cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cauterization is done in many ways, such as:
