que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the back of the abdomen III triangular cauterizations in this form, and it makes good depth and great, and has between each cauterization a space of the size of a finger, and let the cauterization be oil-based.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never cauterize in the middle of the abdomen, because it has four in this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see, if it is cauterized with the cauterization of the circle that we have previously mentioned in the dislocation of the abdomen;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but do it in such a way that the circle contains all the belly, and all the spines are straight.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the manner to do in surgery, when the pain remains in the shoulder and does not reach as far as the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it comes to the thigh and leg, then make two cauteries where the hairs are, and one cautery on the knee four inches above, on the right side a little bit.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauteries be sharp, and let the spines be straight.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the hairs feel that the pain extends to two fingers or near the wrist, then cauterize where it feels the pain three fingers or four at the cauterizing iron called "finger".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if your craft is, then do more of it.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is displaced from the groin to the thigh, then perform a cauterization with a cutaneous or circular cautery, and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you do not cause greater harm and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I myself have seen many who have done cautery on the ankle of the foot, and they let it burn so much that the leg was completely blackened, and the feet as well, and all the flesh was rotten.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a stomach purge causing death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in both parts together, do cauterization on one and the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise say in the cauterization of the loins, in this manner, make such a needle and let it be at the top as large as a small nail or a little less, and let it be inserted between the ribs and let one end insert into the other at a distance equal to the quantity of a new pence.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and they are punctured through two parts, and they are also like needles, and there is one good iron needle.
et c’est li forme:	And this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let them be heated until they are all red and smell like burnt hay, and then place them on the back of the misaligned ribs, and turn them over to the healthy side.
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	And the cauterization is done once the fire has gone out and left for three days.
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	Then apply a poultice of butter, and leave the wound open for ten days.
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the healing of the wound until it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasis says that we use this cauterization little because of its fearful appearance, and few see those who use it.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	And in every way this is the best cauterization, which can suffer, and where it adheres.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cauterizing instrument of burning medicine is such that you make a tool for insertion into the edge of the door, and it is either of rain or iron at one end, and in the height has II us, and between each quantity of the greatness of one dose;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and it is open below and above, and they join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the board of the hipbone on the injured side lying down, and quickly placing your hand on top of the board of the hipbone.
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	Then pour between the two circles of the hot water which is heated by the fire I pot, and let it stand for an hour with slight pressure, and suffer the patient with the heat and burning of the.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it truly has the effect of a burn;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the burn has passed, gently lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip bone gently, and let it rest for three hours, and put on butter until the blackened skin is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it rest for three days until it is healed;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last aid after the treatment of wounds as long as they are healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or leg, make the instrument that you have used in the buttocks increased;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of the hot iron, and I have written about it in treating the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take equal parts of lime and quicklime, and grind them together, and put them in a new earthenware pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or he has one small puncture except that the tip of a razor can pierce through;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put that one in the other, well boiled, and place on alum and chalk and sweet oil until there are two of them above the powders, which you will have well prepared in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it remain until it has descended as much as possible without falling off, then take all of it, and pour it onto charcoal and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And if it is very much, then it should be administered in the form of medicines and cauteries for other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	Because it does work like that, and if there are other medicines that are well-cauterized in the loins such as this and miel anacardi and charcoal with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galiens tells us of a cure where some people were cured of back pain and sciatica, and the louse much, and said that no other cure was done, and that they were healed once when this cure was done, and it was bathed as it is shown hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And in a similar manner, you should take fresh and dry licorice root, and grind it well with a little fat, and put on the loins and thighs and legs where the pain is, and tie it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and he leaves it for three hours and by the amount that the pain does not feel the burning.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then make the patient enter or take a bath until the heart is slightly warmed, and then make him enter or lie down, and the pain will go away completely and be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And it is advised that no one should use such cauterizing medicines unless after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the vein of the arm is cauterized with lead from a goat, it helps a lot.
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and it should be done in this manner by the cautery.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the same and crush it with old oil, and put it on the groove that is between the thumb and the other one called the forefinger.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dry lead from a goat, and putting it in the fire until it becomes charcoal, and putting it on the cloth, and leaving it until it is soaked.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and repeat this, and do not stop doing it until you think that it is approaching the ribs, and that the pain has ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this method of cauterization is called "goat's head cauterization".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain is doubled.
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, or from falling or from impact or from too great evacuation, or from similar expansive cold matter, none of these is worth cauterization, because it is from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary to apply three lines of fetid ointments or similar substances, placed on top of the wound, where the pain is located, using five cauterizing irons or more according to their virtue and quantity that the wound can tolerate.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And it should be made with the cauterizing iron called "spoon".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see, use three or four cauterizing irons according to the middle-claw form of this method.
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Frequently, this disease comes to small children, and the signs of its onset are that they have stiffness in their joints when they move, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you feel a hollowness at the last spinous process of the back and in us, the appearance that comes above the other spinous processes.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and want to heal it, then cauterize with that fire cautery in this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery prepares each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, then cauterize around the spine with that fire cautery touching two or three lines, and the points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After healing the limb as long as it is healthy according to what we have said, and be sure that you do not apply fire cautery in a place where there is a spasm of the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When the pain of joints is due to moisture that has spread to each limb of the body, and when the pain comes in the feet, which is properly called "gout", and when it is caused by cold and cures of medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauteries in this manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make the most of cauterizing around the joint, and let the fire cautery be done in this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a place that you can prick on the face of the foot, then let the cauterizing be done with the whole cautery called "needle".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come to the knees and other joints, and often occur, then let it be cauterized above each knee with three or four fire cautery on each part, throughout the fire cautery;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	and if you have more skill, then do more, but do not exceed your hand beyond what is necessary for the healing of the wound.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend just above the genitals and in the back, administer the cauterization that we have mentioned in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then let it be cauterized around the finger joint with two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	If there is no pain, then make small cuts over each joint and over the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains come from the elbow or shoulder, then cauterize each part, and apply good management to the injury and pain-relieving medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give good governance and purge the humor, it will be healed by the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the toothache
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a fracture occurs in the angle, and the bruises descend to the joints and this is new, then it is necessary that when you see it to treat, that it does not move at all that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he use things that lower the belly, so that the swelling goes down from his stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	After the patient sits on their back between your hands, and you command them to color their spine until the bruise is healed, and you massage it at your discretion, and signify the end of the treatment by a sign that resembles half a circle above the chest.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cauterizing iron in this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	until it is white and sweats scented drops.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then massage the bruises on their limbs.
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And the nurses color their hands so they do not return later.
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And work well on the thighs with the misalignment, and put out of the way the cupping and the leech over the thighs, and the other above the worst one that colors their hands.
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery above the sign at all your fingers, and hold it straight and hold it until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then repeat it another time until you come just to the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and guard subtly that the boil does not burst while you are doing the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that by this means the hairs do not die, or other harm.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And if you do not come to the bone with the cauterization, your work is worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the cautery for children be subtle according to the measure of the eyes, and for large people also large according to their measure;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	After three days, care for the burned area until the scab has formed.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After the care of other remedies until it is healed, and grind the hair 40 times on its back until the wound is well scarred.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it should be covered for a long time, so that the bandages do not stick when he goes to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, give him a well-made bandage, and put it on for another 40 days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And have good rest, that he works little and avoids too much drinking and eating, and too high heat.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he gives this instruction, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will tell you about the cure after cutting into his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When wounds come from other bellies and are known to not be growing anymore, and you see that they are not growing, then apply the fire cautery according to its quantity, and let the third part of the care be.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the care according to what we have said.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And none of the old ones have said that it should be cauterized with the fire cautery at three angles according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	1. But the first sign is the shoulder dropping and make a line across the width of the rent, and another below, and keep your hand on all the cauterizing iron.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	1. But the first cauteries are lighter and more painless.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	1. of ancient pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	1. When pain comes in any limb, whether to fall or to strike, and this pain lasts long, and the medical cure does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cauterizing iron called "poins", and the cauteries should be according to the length of the limb and its smallness and weakness and its strength and its position of twists and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	If it is healthy with the first fire cautery, it is good.
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If it is not healthy with the first fire cautery, then start again with the other cautery above it, for it is usually the case that it should be moved to the member that is closest, because it is necessary that you make the cauteries until the hairs are healthy.
de meselerie	of cauterization
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Cauterization is never used without great help, and simultaneously the disease that comes from the putrefaction of fluids and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	If you see the cautery, take warning if the disease is at the beginning, and if it has been treated according to what we have said in the division, and do not let it spread or stay, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the body, then you must apply several cauteries above the head:
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	and cautery the head at the back and the other towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two above the two horns, and one behind the hairline;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let your hand be so that the cauteries reach the bone, and as long as the scabs come out so that the vapors of the large humors can escape;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and the cautery is applied to the mouse according to what it is supposed to be.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the wound is scattered all over;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it is clearly painful, then you must cautiously cauterize with these cauteries that we have said or chief, and the cauterizing agent in the nostril, and two cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and six cauterizations on the spine of the back, and one on the great buttock and one on the other side, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the hips, and two on the knees, and one on each joint of the hands and feet, and on the grooves of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and guard against the nerves that are above the lower back, so as not to burn them.
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and never perform fire cauterization above the spine, and on the other side of the stomach bone, and on the other side of the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And make sure that the more you perform cauterization, the less help you provide, and move them less.
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	And make sure that the pain does not feel the same as the healthy ones, because the body is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	It should be great and small according to the members and the joints, according to what you will find in the manner of irons.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the limb with flour several times with honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation comes to any limb and is treated with medicines, oils, and plasters, and it does not heal, then perform cauterization above the limb according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cautery enter slightly into the skin.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then apply ointments until they are healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And never cauterize with the hand and the foot and the back, at the end of the nerve that moves the member, and thus if it is broken then it is inflamed.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and do not interfere with anything if they are not knowledgeable about the members and the outlets of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	I'm sorry, I don't understand your request
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the medical knowledge does not help at all, then cauterize with a cautery slightly in front, according to the amount of the skin, until the blister is broken and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	then the cure of flour and lentils with rose oil and plantain leaves, and blood from the colon and blood from the swan, each in equal parts;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let them all be mixed together, and let it be bound with a cloth, and let it be applied to the limb until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of chancre by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When chancre appears at the beginning, and you see it stop growing, if you cauterize it with a cauterizer that seems like a circle, all around the edge of the chancre.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all the wise say that one should make a fire cauterization likewise in the middle of the chancre;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and I do not think it is good, because I believe that it will not be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have never seen it happen once;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the more important thing is that it should be cauterized around, with the cauterant called "circle", as we have said in many cauterants.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the withered who cannot die
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it lingers or due to the excess that it causes or due to the severity of the illness when they are elderly (that is, too old) and they have little blood, or for lack of tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you see it approaching death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	therefore, cauterize around with many small cauterants by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	after leaving it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through the entire cauterization, then heat the cauterization from where it is formed:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauterizer has pierced through, and let the cauterizer be such that the hairs feel afterwards in a similar manner as the course of the porridge is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment until they are completely healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a piece of member, for it twists the members as if the dry reeds would.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in the limb that can suffer from cautery together with fire, then heat the cautery knives very small and large, according to what is needed for the limb or the disease.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After cautery of all parts until you reach all the corruption, and nothing remains of it, that everything that is corrupted be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply a poultice of cauterized herbs on the wounds, suffering with oil until the burned skin is removed, and all corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of wounds, scars are generated.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see after three days that healthy pus does not arise, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if not, then begin the cautery again on what remains of the corrupted parts.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this method has never been treated with medicine in place of fire cautery;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but all fire cauterization is of greater aid, and I have already told the cure of medicine in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take what you have at hand.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the bones that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that the feet by deficiency give birth to a disease called "clubfoot" according to our understanding, and it is a great deformity that makes the foot look like a ball.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauteries for this disease are in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cauterization, and needle cauterization with hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cauterization is such that you heat the cautery as if it were a pen of iron, and it should be made of good iron at the measure that it can pierce the nail of all parts, and that it has thin edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	then put it all heated above the nail, and turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the base of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it stay thus for three hours until it begins to drip blood;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make an ointment of wild, crushed herbs with oil, and leave the ointment on all night, and the splints will be removed and uprooted from their roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound by applying heat until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by previous injuries to the flesh, and often in the hands and feet, then it is necessary that you reapply the fire cautery of hot iron.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in some way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	take a needle of iron or steel, or a quill of vulture, and put it on the splint and the wound, that is to say, pore the verucae.
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	And place the nail across so that it holds everything together, then put a little hot iron, and hold firmly with your hand, and press your hand turning it so that the edge of the nail comes to the root of the nail, and find the hot point deeply near the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and suffer a little from the burning of the hot point for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it like that, and it will all come out at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Then do another one, until you have relieved all those who are in the body, then cure the wounds that cause harm to the heart.
li cure dou trembler	cure of the shaking
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When anyone trembles from cold or a quarter-fever or other, it is necessary that you make four cauteries or four on the spine of the back; one cautery between each spine.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and with fire or pliers, and over the stomach with cauterizing iron;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if it allows the wound to tremble, and the health will quickly recover from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of stinking pustules
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time appears when the body is bathed, or pustules appear that come from large corrupted matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	if it is necessary for the first when they appear that one make cauterization over each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	a fine cauterizing iron of willow wood, of which the tip is held in the fire, or of the root of aristolochia long, or with a lens cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And never cauterize at the beginning when they appear, in this manner, and it cannot grow new ones, but is disrupted from the excess from which they come, and are healthy;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	often there is great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound that comes to the part of the body, or at the incision of the abscess, or in the cauterization of the member, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very painful thing to stop.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	and in any case when it has to do with anyone, you must quickly place your finger on the wound of the vein, and press very tightly until the blood stops flowing out of your finger, and no more gushes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then apply the branding irons of various sizes, both small and large, until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then apply I, whether large or small depending on the wound and where the artery is located, and place the branding iron above that vein where you hold your hand, and keep the branding iron as high as to not leave it uncovered.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if the first one suddenly breaks while you are lifting it above the vein, and the cautery is extinguished, then quickly take the other cautery that is in the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after another until the wound is completely covered.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and watch that you do not burn the tendon that is nearby, and that no other harm comes to the wound.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and ensure that when the wound is cut from the artery, it cannot be completely covered immediately if the artery is large, unless by one of the four methods that we have mentioned.
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	ou by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not yet treated, or by strong pulling with a thread, or by medicines placed above that have the power to stop bleeding;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and then tied and held in place.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever administers tight bandaging of cloth or other things burning above, or similar things, does not benefit unless not.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they do not have any remedy present, then they should place their finger index above the wound of the vein as we have said, and tightly hold it until it is stopped above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and they should not move it, but they should frequently wipe it with cold water until it is very cold and thickened and stopped;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries about what concerns him regarding cautery and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of remedies for tails
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases in which it is necessary to use fire cauterization or fiery medicines, and the questions and causes and instruments and forms of cautery.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I have placed that chapter on the shoulders below the feet, and I will go to this chapter by the same way because it is easier to find what we want.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And therefore when I begin this chapter, it is necessary, dear son, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first of the cauteries, and for this reason it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	when there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you that you should not undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many methods of people come to healing.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if they come from such people who have become so with their disease that they die easily due to the falsehood of their disease, and the greatness of their misfortune;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one should fear these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And among these, there are those who give you sense, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am grainy";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is stubborn.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	You should only consent to those who come to you with this manner, but put more careful consideration in your honor than in your desire, and do not open rashly, but wisely of what you are certain, and which you have taken and lost;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prediction and indication in the treatment of your ailments for health to be converted;
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and it will help you to acquire good reputation, and glory, and memory of the long term.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, Our Lords give you good understanding and truth, and if you wish to breathe from the holy inspiration of his hand, indeed.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	I have ordered you to write this chapter by examining other chapters, according to what is before the chapter on cauteries, which I have previously described from head to foot, so that you may find it more easily.
dou chief plein d’aigue	full of sharp
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is said that this disease often occurs in children at birth, and when the neck of the child is held too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and it never occurs for no reason that one has not been.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease except in children, and all those that I have seen have died;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and therefore it seems to me that it is better to abandon this work in these treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	I saw a child who was complaining of sharp pain, and the head was swelling each day until it could not be supported.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and believed it was so much moisture that he died, and this moisture is gathered outside the bone above the symphysis, between the jaw and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the work is such that if the moisture is between the jaw and the bone, and the abscesses are small, then you should make a wide incision into the head;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as ours, until the moisture drains out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and now the form of the spotlight:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more extensive, and the abscess is larger, make two incisions in the shape of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is outside the bone, and you see the signs of the commissures of the head opened on each part, and the sharp pain when you press it with your hand inside, and it does not return to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then it is necessary that you make three cuts in the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, remove all the moisture.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After straining the cuts with linen and powders, and put wine and oil, and leave it thus for five hours;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then release it, and treat the wound with compresses and counter-irritants, and leave the head strained equally, and give the patient dry meat to eat until the member is comfortable and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another way of incision is that you look at the size of the abscess and the gathering of pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for it is never there.
aucune fois derrier;	never behind.
aucune fois en destre;	never to the side.
et aucune fois en senestre.	and never to the other side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Measure then where the abscess is open and the gathering of pus, and make the cut according to what you have the ability to do.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and be careful not to cover the artery.
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and bring a little blood, so that the hairs do not die from the drainage of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	I'm sorry, I don't understand
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When it happens to someone with a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or the pupil, and the disease is ancient, and medical treatment does not help much, then the cure is to cauterize with what covers the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is therefore necessary, when you see them coping, to make the hairs grow back on their heads.
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After that, he rubs the affected area with a rough cloth until the arteries appear, then holds the hairs steady against all the cloth.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look at where the blood flows out, and the veins on both sides are behind the ears, and they are not yet restored.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then sign the veins with a sharp needle, then cut both sides of one inch, until the vein comes just to the bone, and this should be through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, press the lint away from the artery and cover it above, cutting as much as it should be through the middle.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, the blood spurts continuously outwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open when felt, it is necessary to measure the quantity of space at three digits, then drill into the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and the amount of blood that needs to be let out is six cubic centimeters, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on what the patient can bear and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains above the bone pointed, and if the gauze that was applied does not come out, then strain the wound and bind it, and apply the ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	Of the head
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When an ancient headache comes, and the catarrh is sharp, due to the moisture of tears and chills in the temples and old age and similar things, and it is treated with methods of medical cures and nothing seems to help, then we should cauterize the arteries of the temples, as we have said.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of extracting them is such that the hairs of his temples face the bad ones, and listen to the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is quickly restored only in some men who are too thin;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is restored, hold the neck with some cloths, then rub the limb with some rough cloth, and raise the limb with hot water until the artery opens clearly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spoon of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then gently scrape the skin until you reach the artery, then cut it at the top with pincers, and remove it well from all the bands that are outside of each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the artery is thin, turn it back to the tip of the needle, then cover that part according to the amount of the two needles.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not covered, it will not heal completely.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And draw out one drop of blood from the sixth vein, just enough to three drops.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, it is necessary to tie it in two lengths of a strong silk thread, double thickness, so that no blood comes before the healing of the wound, and no bleeding occurs.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cover the excess between the two knots in the same hour, and then, if you see, if the patient is cauterized with the cauterizing iron just to the bone until the needles are covered.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the mortal work, if the pains are not accompanied by fever and he has a hot constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cautery is used to finish the moistures:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	Therefore, it is of greater help against moistures.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	Or it is necessary for the extraction of arrows that one fills the wound with old cotton and places bandages well made;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they are removed, one should apply dry medicines that cause heat and bandages until they are healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if without cutting the artery as much as you work, then one must quickly cover it with a cauterizer, or one fills the wound with vinegar and hold it in one's hand that the uncut part is not soaked.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	and if you do not have this present, put it on the limb as much as the joint should not be frozen, and raise the limb from high cold water until the joint is constantly, and it should be stretched as it should.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	and what is more fluid and lighter in the extraction of the artery is that you cauterize the vein with this cautery cutting from two parts, but the cutting should be well spaced to last longer in their heat.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	When the instruments are too tight, it holds less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And it should have between the two knives one inch of space, and then when you have stopped the bleeding from both veins, and you melt the hot iron on top until it comes just short of the bone, and cover the vein in two parts;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they are spaced apart between the two shoulders because there is no doubt about this cauterization all in all.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and it is the form of the cauterization:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	when the tears of the eyes are flowing down from the veins that are above the back of the head, and it does not benefit from any medical treatment that is done, and you see the face of the patient become twisted, and feels as if there is a trembling.
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and they are held and moistened so much that the hairs of the papers are burned, and the papers are scorched by the heat of the tears, if there is a need for this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they called the ancient "healer of contusions," and you should do this for the patient who has this disease, to let his hairs grow on the front, then make three cuts evenly along the length of the front;
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and either one of the cuts as if two are too low in front, and the others two on the ribs above the papers, and be careful not to incise the arteries that are above the ribs;
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	and move your hand away from the continuation of the two mandibles, and each wound the quantity of three drops through the joints;
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	and have prepared a piece of sponge and plenty of cloths to absorb the blood, then boil the syringe full of two parts of this mixture:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the incision which is made from the temple just above the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	and scrape all that is between the two cuts to the entire surface of the face which is above the bone, then make another cut from the same incision towards the other second, and then extract this syringe.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you insert the tool called "cultellaire" into the first cut, it is very sharp on one side and blunt on the other, and its shape is:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the sharp edge of the tool towards the cheek and the blunt side towards the bone, and push it until it reaches the other cut.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cover all the vessels that descend from the head as far as the eyes until the incision is continued as far as the surface of the face, and then make another cut from the same incision towards the other side;
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	and then strain out the blood evenly, and express the joint for the blood taken.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	then place a piece of clean, old cloth in each wound, and apply poultices made of flour mixed with wine, oil, and vinegar, and make sure that abscesses do not form.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then apply a new bandage to the wound, and apply a large amount of fresh garlic, then use the healing salve with rose oil, and other remedies to treat the wound, until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	repetition of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When using the fire cauterizer, you will see the eyes tense and small, and weakened, and the papers burned.
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	and the hairs prick, and when they are shaved, there is great pain in the forehead, and the hairs are discharged.
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	therefore avoid these accidents that those matters and that cautery do not come from many wounds, and the healing that is, if it is this.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you command the patient to turn his head back, then make a deep cut across the forehead, and another one wide at the top of the nose.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	and begins from the wound on the right temple to the left temple, and the incision just to the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and avoid your hand from the nerves of the temples that move at the wound;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, soak up all the blood with a sponge, and then clean between the two lips of the wound and put old cloth, and apply linen;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then place bandages soaked in wine and oil above, and guard against abscess.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	When it is removed, it is necessary that you rub the bone until it begins to burn like charcoal, then treat with things that cause sweating, which make one perspire.
En teil maniere:	In a similar manner:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flour and four parts of mustard, and make an ointment.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	And administer it in these wounds to cause sweating throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	of ear obstruction
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	All that which drips into our ears is one of the four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	or grains, or beasts, or arrowheads of stone or similar things like iron.
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	if seeds, such as beans, peas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	or things that flow down, such as honey and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When it enters the ear as a stone or other thing that does not fit well in the ear, it does not grow in the ear, so put the ear to the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, if any drop of purple oil or hemlock oil drips, then moisten extraction.
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	and the patient's condition is made to vomit, and he stops his nose when he vomits, and puts cloth or wool inside the ear.
et estent l’oreille au desus.	and the ear is held upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Often, this treatment causes.
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come up, then moisten extraction with delicate tweezers, of which this is the shape:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If they jump as far as possible with pins, it is good.
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	If not, then apply gentle pressure extraction at the subtle groove of the small double-joint.
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	And if they do not jump by that, then make a rain cloud and press the top of the cloud onto the ear canal or opening of the ear, and stop the wax inside the ear with soft candle so that it cannot enter with the cloud.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	Then remove it carefully, as it often comes out like we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	And if it does not come out in that manner, then take some gauze and wrap it around the eyes, and put any instrument that is sharp to cut through wax, and put a small amount of cotton inside.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the gland above the stone or whatever it is, and drain it.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if she does not drain from all these things that we have said, then quickly cut open the ear as if it is an abscess, and blood flows, and spasms.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	And the manner of the cut is that you first suck out the pus from the ear canal, and then draw out the blood according to the measure of its virtue, then place the pus between your hands and turn the ear upwards, and make a small cut at the base of the ear at the grease or where it depends.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the knife be as sharp as a crescent moon, until you reach the stone, then chip away according to your ability, and suck it vigorously into your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and the cure until they are healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if it is small and swells up, administer extraction;
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	and if it cannot be removed, then administer the following subtle remedy according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and administer incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not make a mistake when you think the grain is moist due to earwax, until you have made many pieces of it;
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	then extract it with delicate forceps and suction, as we have said, so that the extraction is aligned.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the ear therefore that is blocked, it is appropriate to use the blowing of the nose of the condition first, and widen the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let it lie flat across the ear itself or where the sharp pain is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If it jumps out due to the sky, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	if not, take many needles according to the length of your thread and thin, and heat them slightly in the fire;
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and insert the hairs one by one through an opening in his ear, and go up from there. from the other foot, and pierce with another needle above the needle that is in the ear;
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not stop piercing with needle after needle until the sharp one has passed through entirely, and thus it will pass through entirely;
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	If you see, take a reed, and blow one of the shoulder blades into the ear, and the other hold with fire until the most flexible reed is burnt.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	Then make another of the other joints until the sharp edge is all gone, as we have said in the stone.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of the beast, if it is small, like a mouse and similar things, treat it as we have said in the division.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	But if it is of large size, so that one can feel it, then minimize the extraction of pins.
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	And the least thing to remove is what is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In extracting worms from the ears, if you are unable to cure as we have described in the division and treatment of distillations, and the cure does not help, then you should look into the ear using sunlight.
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	If there are no worms, then use thin forceps to extract them; if they do not appear, then take the form of the tool that is used for this purpose.
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And be narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And use the most subtle tool in the ear according to the amount of pain caused by the worm, then it is successful for the entire tool.
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Do this often until all the worms are out.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey to exit, then bend the needle around the neck of the cotton as I have said in the stone.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	And if they do not succeed as we have said, then administer distillations that the ancients have experienced in the opening of veins, and you will find them where to treat distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if you distill your oils and medicines into the ear of this instrument, as you see in this form:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And it should be made of silver or brass, with small holes below to pour and above to pour out.
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	And to press within the distillation of the well-made brass instrument for this, and if you see take a razor and wrap it around the tip evenly with cotton.
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	then pour your oil or juice into the ear, and whatever you see in the canal, and the canal should be in the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	then press the cotton into the toothbrush and press your hand firmly until the oil is dripped or moved out of the ear.
