et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And the medicines are applied, and the plaster is placed in high molten and moistened.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if it is above its shoulder, and you can place it even, then alleviate as we have said in the living child.
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if you cannot do it, then tear it by pieces, and leave nothing of the second one.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, alleviate as we have said in abscesses which come into the marsh.
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if blood comes out, then place it in acute restriction, and alleviate other cures.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	I saw a woman in whose belly an infant had died, then consulted the other about that one, and he also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, some abscesses appeared in the groin, and they swelled up so much that they burst, and then began to cause great pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the patient, and I thought for a long time, and could not stop the bleeding.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied strong adhesive bandages, and then some bones were exposed, and after some time others appeared.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very surprised because the belly does not have any bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that it must be the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I looked at the wound, and in the meantime, I treated the bones, until the woman was much better.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and it is tied with a long piece of cloth around the shoulder, and it is placed in place with a little bandage of the body.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not remembered this chapter except for the reason that, when the masters find an unusual thing, they know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	bring the marsh to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Then comes the form of the pressor, which is used to apply pressure;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and it is applied to the two joints of the elbow.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horn should be more subtle than the restraint, and it should be made of metal or wood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and its mouth should be two inches wide, and the edge of the trees should be long, and one and a half palms.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs, there are two joints of this same kind, which are firm in one and the other, half a palm length or a little more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are closed in the mouth of the jaw when turning the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, of a more subtle and lighter appearance, is made of flat or boxwood, according to the appearance of nails.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has two joints like these, as you see, half a palm length, and they should be wide.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the jaw opening with all the instrument, then place the woman on the bed, the feet still and the legs open, then close the two joints together in the jaw, and hold the head of the instrument outside between her teeth.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then use your hand on all the instruments, as you have evenly made the pliers, according to the quantity that you saw open the mouth of the marsh, until the bail does what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all above, and are multiplied in their likenesses;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when the mirrors have them arranged, so much the faster they work, and so much higher they are to men for their quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despise the instrument that you have not prepared, because their necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second one is held by the childbirth, it is necessary that you command the pain to hold her hair, and then make her spit out the condition, and your hands at the mouth and the nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps for heaven, well then.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If heaven does not, then take the pot, and make a syrup or coverlet, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the throat, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia lignea, and centaury.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or any of them, should be cooked or boiled over the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	then put a cloth or syrup from the pot in the mouth of the throat, and the steam comes out into the throat;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make her spit it out, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second joint is broken harshly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she remains after this treatment, and is not better, then command the midwife to moisten her right hand with semolina or musk oil, and then blow into it, and give the second dose.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she has found it, grasp and extend it gently and straight, so that the husband does not cut during extraction.
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But move it slightly to the right and left, and then pull it out.
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes and dislodges.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the husband's mouth is too narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of vomiting and fumigation of herbs.
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	And if it is not all of what we have said, then remember to not pull.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is recommended that what is at the mouth of the marsh, you tie to the belly of the woman, then smear with a healing ointment made from four ingredients.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it will not rot and return, and will come soon.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	But if it rots when a bad smell comes to the stomach and head, and causes pain.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Then you should apply smoking treatments to this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have experienced fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument used to smoke the woman during retention of flowers and the secondine is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it appears like glass, and they place the head under the natural heat, and the others widely over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and either the fumigations over the coals, and the wart until it is burned, and start another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who have not yet reached the foundation pierced, but it has been stupefied by some subtle syrup:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	therefore the midwife should pierce that syrup at its proper time, and not pierce it too early with sharp instruments, and cleanse the wound so it does not touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then place on the wound a soft cloth in wine and oil, then the healing ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not reset, put or plug a splint, and let it lie for some time, and be supported as the child wants to go into the rooms.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And never comes this stoppage of pus from a wound or abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	if it is necessary to drain that pus:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if it is treated, as we have said of the swine's dung.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from below the foundation are nodular and thicker than those that come above the foundation, or in the space between two parts, if there is one fistula or more.
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when that nodular one is old, it works and thickens with moisture to become white or subtle blue, and those fistulas are never persistent.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and are known by the fact that there is outflow or vomiting when the pain makes an outflow, and sometimes some verses.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if there are fistulas that protrude into the bladder, and protrude into half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach into the sacrum, and into the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows the fistula passing through the basement, and not passing through:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you pierce your own index or base, and pierce a thin needle of silver or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if he has tortuosity, if you put a thin layer of pitch, or horsehair, until you feel the pitch or hair at your fingertips;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and it does not come out with puncture or sweatiness or vinegar, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	so that it does not pierce through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hurry to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is persistent near the bladder or near a urinary tract, if it allows urine to pass, and cannot be cured by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced up to the joint of the elbow, then the pitch comes out to the skin;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no tortuosity and the pain is internal, then it is that it is inside, and there is no medicine or treatment by fomentation;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in these fistulas, there is no cure but labor, and the vanity of those who try to treat them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In that one which is not very deep and not very ancient, with hope of healing by fire, as I have experienced, and it is that the pains are hidden between your hands on its back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and the patient's legs up to their knees, and its knees bent towards its belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then pour water or mud, if there is twisting, until you clean it out.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the pain is felt around the foundation, then you must insert your finger, as if it has pierced the tent.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and it is discovered or you feel between your teeth whether it is the tongue or the throat, then spit out that it has passed.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if not, there is no way to heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that one can heal almost anything, but this rarely happens.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the aid that is done, if it is to heat the subtle cauterizer according to the width of the fistula, as it is said before.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and the whole bottle is placed in the fistula, until it reaches the bottom.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and do this two or three times, until you know that these charred pieces are burned, which resemble a barb of an arrow.
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the treatment of broken bones in butter, until that bone is set, then the treatment of burns with heat and sealing.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus healthy, it is well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If not, nothing else can be healed.
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if it is not healed between, and does not perforate just at the base, and between the tent and the wound, a thick layer of charcoal or ash, and you see the fistula that leads to the cure underneath the covering.
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If the cover of the beginning of the fistula, and it is stuck before the tent, and then the cauterization after, until it reaches the top of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and he will be delivered from the tent, and fall.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then one must believe those charms that seem like a quill of a goose, and not remain without them.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if you cannot straighten it, and cut between you and the work, then cauterize with fire or medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery brings together two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, the burning of these charms applied, and the stopping of blood and the drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the treatment of tents torn or broken in pieces, until the eyes are filled with blood, and then the charms burned in the eye.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then the treatment of wounds infected with boils, soaked in hard charcoal, and the dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes from just above the foundation, and is distant from the body, then press on the top or base, and look for it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between II is the cloth or the sweat or the charcoal, where it is close to being pierced, there should be no other means than the administration of one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut it from the bottom up, or if you can, put bandages and treat it as first aid;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not remove too quickly from the front, so that you do not cover the foundation which holds the foundation, and it comes out through the way of excretion;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	If by chance it is healed, or you remove that covering and the wound then it is cut above the foundation, or by tent or by other instrument appointed;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then monitor that char which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	then study to restore the wound, and to delay the fistula in the part before the foundation:
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is a lighter thing at the misalignment.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas are in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	and when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is out of the foundation below the skin above, then take a tent perforated at the top in this form:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And push the thread into the fistula, and push the probe through the entire thread in the fistula until it reaches the top.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is lost on the edge of the foundation beneath, then hold the thread of that which is plugged, so that you can pull your own or the foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and trace the head of the thread, and gather the two ends together, and hold them against each other, and let it lie for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it not once, until the thread covers those charges that are between two, and stick.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed and clean.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not open, try to puncture it in all the ways you can, unless it is too far back.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it does not matter to make the placement cover if it is too far back, and then treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spinous bone that is made into a fistula is very sharp and one-sided;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand, not, because we do not know how to handle what we should not handle, as you see here.
des emorroydes	Des emorroides
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	There are two main methods:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Or they are within the foundation, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and in this case, blood clots, and there are one or more, and they are under the foundation and at the base of the foundation.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that are underneath have little moisture, and they are cut or a little sharp or a little blood, and they have the color of the blood.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment of those who have them within the foundation is that you command the patient to urinate in other rooms until the foundation is full and it appears.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, you can hold it with pliers, or hold it with your finger, then cut it at its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if they cannot hold it with their fingers due to its moisture, take it with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of linen.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	And hold it with your two hands, then cut it, and powder the wound with any hot powders that are in the cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize it as it is written in the book of cauterization, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	And if the base cannot be lifted, then cleanse the wound with a sharp and biting clyster to remove what is stuck at the base, so that it can come out openly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	When the hairs are pricked at their base, and if they are thick and strong from the root, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And you should hold them with your fingers or pliers, and cut them off, then treat them as we have said, until they are healed, and do not fear the incision with iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	If it is necessary to stitch the wound in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a thick thread, and wind it around a needle, and then pull the thread from above and make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread away from the needle, and if it is wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and hold the thread firmly, then pull the thread, and extract the needle, and do so with all the others, and leave it for the excess of the blood.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place above the foundation a cotton bandage soaked in rose oil or wax, and place above the foundation, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let it remain until they heal, and when they are healed, apply ointment and other treatments until they are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	dried and withered from the base
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	often found dried and withered in the intestines, and due to constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine does not help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	If it is necessary that you apply the scraping of a spatula or your finger above, which does not allow it to become moist.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then the healer, as much as it should be, as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if he cannot cure, then start the scraping stronger than before, until it is clean, and be scorched.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the healer, as much as it should be clean.
dou fremit	high fever
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Mice is a small appearance cut in front of the chest, and goes up much into the front.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And never the trace of the frost, and the feeling is like death from shivering, and comes throughout the body, and more in the hands than any other part.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the healer so that you take a quill of a goose pen, or a pen of vulture very strong, and put that quill on the shivering, until the circle prevents the shivering all around.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand all around the wound until you remove everything inside the swelling, and put it in a pot, and extract the swelling from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, do this according to the form of a rain or iron dog, and it is subtlely pushed out and pulled up:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce, to keep the two together, and to press.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see, if you cauterize the swelling, as it is before or in the chapter of cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the splint
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Never use a silver paste, or an alloy of lead, or melted tin, or tin filings.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And never use these small and large instruments, according to those which you will bring.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, those who are to be treated in the care of children and those who are weak and painful, are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of this plaster is small and large if it is above wide, or the belly is tied according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is a discharge or the belly is tied, as you see, and the wound is inside, pierce.
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	And say to one of the two sides, "II", and on the other side, "I".
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	And let the belly or the one who applies the medicines use a bladder of beast or parchment, and pierce all around with small holes, and have between each hole "I" amount of space, then fill these holes with one thread of thread twisted in X or around, and gather the belly as if it were a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	And when the medicine is inside, if the thread has the instrument in front of a strong thread, then suture;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	And it is the form of a circle.
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and grease the head of the suture with oil or a similar substance, then fill it lightly;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	then the ministers pour water into both of his hands together, until it is completely clear, then remove the cyst, and relieve the pain in his legs by applying a poultice to the affected area, and if the wound allows, let it heal as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	and if he sleeps a whole night through, it is a greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you give the clyster in the disease of diarrhea, and the medicine wants to come out quickly, then restart it as long as it is healthy.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if his hemorrhoids are at the base or in an abscess, then the cyst should be removed as delicately as possible for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the shape of the delicate cyst when the skin is stretched:
des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have said in the section on wound care;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	we will tell you about the treatment of hands and medicine, according to completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are different according to what they are made of, and according to the limbs or wounds that are made, and from what they are made of.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things that are done to make wounds are by piercing with a needle, and cutting with a sword or dagger, or lance or staff or siette, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or they are done according to the laws of the body, such as a wound that pierces through the neck, or head, or foot, or belly, or liver, and similar members;
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	and I will tell you the treatment of each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, because its memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans, et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut:	I say that when a simple wound comes or the bone is not broken, be careful if it is of penetration of an arrow or similar things, and the skin is completely torn and is large, and you slightly doubt of abscess:
si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	if the wound is recently clean of blood, and the cleaning is on the injured side instead:
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and avoid the pain of overeating wine and large meats.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to clean, let him eat soft meat, and not drink wine, and do not change his diet:
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	And apply to the wound, if pus arises and comes out, cotton moistened in rose oil alone or in vinegar stiptic.
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	And if there is no pus, apply above the wound, if it is fresh and full of blood, and it does not move due to air, powder, which I will say a little later.
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound has moved, apply some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like a sword cut and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together by stitches, then bring them together by sewing, as I will say in wounds of the belly, from sewing.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope;	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and can be moved, and does not hold but only at one point, then cover it.
puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir, et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	Then heal the wound with medicine, and restore hardness in the flesh instead of skin, and command the patient to eat large foods, such as tests and cooked grain, like chicken, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you suspect bone fracture, and it is not to the bone, then cover the entire wound, and pour boiling water, then heal.
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there is an artery in the wound or vein, without cutting, and it cannot be stanched by medicines, then suture the artery, and if you suspect a fracture, dislocate it with a thread.
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	And if it does not improve, then cauterize.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere:	And if these wounds are small and simple, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	and you put this powder that smells like what the wound has lost.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est:	And the manner of the powder is as follows:
pren encens une partie;	take a part of incense;
sanc de dragon II parties;	blood of dragon two parts;
chalz vive III parties, et le poudre subtilment, et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	chalk alive three parts, and the powder finely, and fill the wound, and let it settle and join to all its blood;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle;	and then bind it well, and let it remain without swelling;
car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	for one does not use medicine until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And one should never use chalk alone when one does not have frankincense or dragon's blood, but that the wound has moved.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound has moved, immediately in its place, do not put any other of this powder;
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but put on some digestive ointments, or flour of barley made of honey and water, until it is healed;
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then perform other treatments until they are healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the broken bone comes with the wound, and it is small, then strain it with fine needles.
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you what to do after the fractures of the main ones.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound of the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound comes from the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between this and the main wound, but if the neck nerves or the artery is cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerves, there is no other method than to let the care, and not put anything restricting, for it harms nerves and makes them recede.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	and do not put anything sharp on the wound, for the substance of nerves is cold, and the continuation of it is with the brain, which is one of the highest members.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce, et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	but if the medicine is not suitable, such as chalk washed in sharp vinegar, and mixed with rose oil, and the wound cleaned similarly in sharp vinegar, and other stones according to this manner, and moistened with warm water.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, then bandage it well and treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and have been cut and filled with blood, then pierce or lower the limb.
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	And if the artery is cut and blood flows out, then open it, clean it, and cauterize as necessary.
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va, si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	And if the arrow from the throat is cut, or the wound is deep, and the vein is kept, by which the meat goes, then cut the arrow above the back of the throat, but do not touch the throat, but put it back according to its natural shape.
et puis l’estraint avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then gradually stretch it, and leave it for some time, then treat the wounds until they are healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression in the bone, if desired;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse, et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and if there are pieces of bone, remove them all if possible, and those you cannot remove, leave until the wound heals, then disinfect and align the bone;
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	and if the wound is fresh, apply the powder that I have mentioned.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if he has bone in the wound and there is a fistula, then treat it as I have described in his chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound from an arrow or a sword
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne:	If it is a spear or dagger, and the wound is deep, look to see if there is any sign of wind blowing through the wound:
saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	There are times when the wound is mortal;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont, et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and if it is not deep and fresh with all its blood, then in the first hour do not put powder on it or tie it up for the blood that does not coagulate and returns to the heart, and causes pain;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie II fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment and tie it twice a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor, et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie III jors, ou IIII, ou plusors;	and if you do not have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to absorb the moisture, and let the pain sleep on the wound for three days, or four, or more;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’estraingnemens d’alainne;	if no spasm comes, nor trembling of the heart prevents it.
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good positions, cut out the wound.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Treat the wounds and other treatments, until they are healed.
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule;	And if it cannot heal and work, then cut out the fistula.
si la cure si com on doit.	if the treatment is as it should be.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or dagger cut, and it is simple, or worse, at the back, then treat what is in front.
s’elle est grans, de cousture;	if it is large, of stitching.
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it is small, of powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and in it has chipped pieces, if it wounds, and the fragments if they are not removed.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not removed, then let the wound fester, and it will align the extractions.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other members, it is up to judgment as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	belly rupture
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The dislocations of the abdomen are large and medium and small.
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	of the great wound never leaps out the intestine, or the nerves of the intestines, by which the intrusion of others.
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the seam is more painful, and it is never worse than the small wound because one must not reset the intestines unless they are put back in their proper place.
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell quickly when they feel the cold, and they must not be reset unless they are put back in their proper place, and because it is better to have the small wound, for one must not twist the intestines back to their proper place as with others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And there are four ways to treat a hernia of the belly:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common seams are in the belly seam, and the seam of other wounds of the body and two other private seams are common to other wounds.
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	And all ways they are more proper with the seam of the belly, and I will say one by one and explain each.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small, and nothing of the intestine is protruding, and there is no other thing to remove, it is best to return it by one of the two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or by the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because the intestine is inflated by the heat.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is hot, warm it in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	moisten a sponge or some dry cloth only in cold water, or cook in cold, sour and salty water and vinegar, and boil the intestine until it is softened;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And never once has this wine been restricted, and it is believed that it can cause swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling disappear, if the intestines are dry or high and painful, because by this means the entry is soon achieved.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, then make a small incision in the wound with the instrument used to remove the splinters.
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	And the first care is believed that the wound, that we should not cut without great necessity.
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And this is the instrument for cutting:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	If it is cut within the crown and not without, and see its shape.
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound is enlarged, and the intestine jumps out, if you can put it back according to its natural form in its own place, because this is good.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is wide, and it is in the lower part of the abdomen, then you should place the patient on their back, and raise their legs higher than their head.
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And if it is in the lower part of the abdomen, then place the head and the foot higher than the other parts, and also if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts, then place the injured part higher than the other.
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus you should manage as I said in large and medium-sized wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, apply what you have prepared, then place your hands between them and administer ointments that cover the entire wound and close the lips.
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of stitching, and it is that you grip an needle or more, according to the quantity of the width of the wound, then leave some space at the edge of the wound, and sew with a needle or if it has good thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	And pierce the two needles through the two pieces of leather, which is outside the leather inside, until you make it pierce from that part, and gather the two needles together four times.
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	Then, wrap the string of a double-threaded needle around the needle of II parts, then evenly assemble the two pieces of the wound, and then leave one finger's space, and make another stitch.
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Then, tie the wound with a thread as you did with the first needle, and do not stop doing this according to what you know about needles until the entire wound is closed.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And let the needles be medium-sized, between thin and thick, for thin needles cover the entire wound, and too thick ones cannot enter well.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore, it is necessary that they be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and it is not advisable to place the needles too far from the back of the horn and the skin, so they do not pierce and open the wound before sewing.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and then cover the wounds of the needles, so they do not pierce the pain at night, and place bandages or cloths on the wounds of the needles to hold them until the wound is sewn.
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	and this method of sewing with needles is more convenient for small wounds, because it requires only one or two needles.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second method of sewing is common, and it is that you gather the two pieces of skin and the two pieces of sinew together with one needle and a strong thread in the middle.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have perceived these four together, then reset the needle at the part where you began, in the manner that one counts the threads.
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and put space between each stitch the thickness of a thread.
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	This stitch heals the man, and I sewed a wound that one had in the abdomen, which was cut by a knife, and was the wound more than one palm of great, and it pierced the intestines well two palms of great, and was the wound in the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I brought back the intestine after it had been there for 24 hours, and the wound was dressed after 15 hours, and I treated it, and it healed.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And the master had judged that he would die, and it was a miracle;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	and did not heal it with ointment, for I was in a place where none were found, nor any medicine.
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	and I placed moss on the wound twice a day, and washed it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	Or I will tell you the two proper methods of sewing:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	take the needle, and the thread from the part behind, inside.
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	when it has pierced the center correctly, then insert the needle at the head or where you put the thread, and make it pierce from the other side of the part inside.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And the understanding of this sewing is that you should sew as the tailor does with furs, and leave one side of the seam once, and then bring it back from the other side, until the sewing is completely finished.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of sewing, which Galen describes properly, is such that anyone does, who assemble the two parts naturally together and apply one of the main sides of the seam to the other main side, in a similar manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Take a needle or the main point of the awl close by, and pierce only that side, and leave the two sides of the seam;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	then turn the needle, and pierce it through the part in front of this from below, as the two heads of the shoulder.
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	then pierce the other two through the part in front of this from below, in the two other heads of the shoulder that are on the other side.
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	and this is the most common method of sewing and it is the deadliest.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	If anyone says this word, and no one bears witness, then you should sew the belly with two needles, where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and you should put one needle from one side, and the other from the other, in the manner of those who sew corroies.
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and when the fracture is in the belly, it is more painful than other abdominal injuries.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgments of the wound are such as the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and when you clean the fresh wound of all its pus, and as soon as the doctor has moved it, if you remove the intestine and the cloth:
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then put on powdered charcoal, and if the doctor has moved it, then put on any ointment that is present until the wound heals.
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	and bind the cloth, and make sure the sutures are sound, and the muscle:
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as you would with others, until they are healed.
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And if you do not have medicines, then place this immediately, as soon as it begins to bleed, a soft cloth, and shake it twice a day until it is healed.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you have no other use of medicine in many positions where the wounds are simple;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And if you doubt that the wound does not communicate with the main members, then it is necessary to rub another light oil of mild heat, or in red oil, and place it inside the angles, and remove from the bones;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	And if he feels pain or putrefaction in the abdomen, and often occurs, then apply black wine grape clasters, and immediately if the putrefaction comes to the intestines.
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And puncture it, and scrape what when it is the large intestines, it is lighter to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine called "jeun" cannot be healed when it is empty, because of the plants that are in it, and the subtlety of all the body, and its approach to the nature of the nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the pus jumps from the wound, then put it back as the intestines, while it is fresh.
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	And if it is old and becomes green or black, then you must tie the limb that is black, because there are veins and arteries.
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	Then, cut the tissue that is between the joints, and place the two fingers hanging from the part away from the wound to the side of the injury to align the extraction when the bone shatters, and the wound opens.
de la routure dou boueil	of the breaking of a boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestines are torn, and the wound is small, if it can be restored to some people, because I have seen that some men were gutted from their belly by a lance.
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And the wound was on the right side of the stomach, and it became a fistula, and in it there was excrement and feces.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I placed medicine according to what I could, and did not stop treating it until it was healed, and the wound closed.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him suture, I doubted that the hairs had not harmed his stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	but there was no harm, but he remained in better conditions, and fed and watered;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and they said no experts that when he had a small wound in the intestine, that he should be tied in such a way:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	take thick threads, then gather the lips of the wound, and when the thread has opened the mouth, if it puts it above the two lips, so that it holds his mouth open;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	and then cover the head, and it holds so that he cannot move, then put the other thread in the same way as before, until the wound is completely closed;
et cout la plaie.	and bandage the wound.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	If the sharp object enters the intestine and causes no harm to the patient, and it can be sutured with a thin thread that is taken from the intestine of an animal, in such a manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	take the tip of this intestinal thread that is very sharp, and then tie it to the tip of this thread with a thin linen thread, then pull the thread through the needle, and sew the intestine, and bandage the wound;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	and this method of suturing is no other than according to the way of faith and hope.
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	If the wound is large and wide, even when it is in one of the internal organs, there is no remedy or health, only subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	of fistula or that it is
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	All wounds or abscesses, when they become covered, are universally called "fistula", and specifically when they are cut open and reopened.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And the fistula is along the spine, a hard and white tube, where there is no pain, and it is as sharp as the quill of an owl.
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And never in clear bowels, and sometimes thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	And never too thin, and sometimes enough.
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	And I have spoken about this in the division of wounds, that every wound that is not healed, and there is no char, it is only due to one of the EIGHT causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	It is to know, by the smallness of blood or flesh;
ou por sa malice;	or for its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	or because there is hard carrion inside, and on the lips, that does not let blood rise;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	or because there is too much pus.
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or because the bones are broken, and the matter is of bad quality.
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or because the medicine is not good in the cure.
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption is like a plague.
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or because the property in the region is late for digestion, and late for health, and expelled by nature.
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	where there are veins or bones
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the treatments of remedies in that section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	It is necessary for me to inform you of the treatment of fistulas that are made by the work of hands.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	It is said that fistulas can occur in all parts of the body.
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	for there are fistulas that come to large veins, and arteries, and nerves, or to the face, or to the intestines, or to the bladder, or to any of the ribs, or to the spine of the back, or to any joint of the hands or feet.
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it comes to the proper property of the main member, and similar ones.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all such wounds are of great suffering, and there is only labor and ignorance.
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And if there is no such wound that does not come just below the joint that I have said, and you have faith in the cure, and you know how to do it, take a tent of tin or iron, if the wound is straight, if it is curved.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	And if the wound is twisted, then circle it with a thin tent of linen, for the linen will stick to the twists.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	And if the wound is perforated and you cannot well encircle it with tents, then cauterize one of the perforations, for the moisture will pass from one perforation to another, and cleanse it.
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	then carefully apply your skill, to know if there is bone or tendon, and if it is sharp at the edge, and ask the patient well about the pain he feels when you press with your hand, and where he feels it.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	and when you know truly where the bone or bone is, and if it is far from the joint, or tendon, or artery, or vein, or any of the limbs that I have told you, then cut according to what I have told you, and remove the fractured pieces and the charred parts that are inside;
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	and then the cure until it is healed, and if the fistula is well positioned at the right place, then you must cut across, as much as you can, then put soft bandages in medicine water, and squeeze them at the top of the fistula, until the medicine corrodes the excess that remains at the bottom.
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then I apply clean ointment to the wound, until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	and if it is not healed by that, then cauterize it as we have said, and if the bone is corrupted by a fistula, then extract it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If the vein or nerves do not harm the principal members, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	and if the bone is exposed, and there is corruption and blackness, then remove as much of the corruption as possible, then apply clean ointment to the wound until it is healed.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	and if it is not healed, and remains as before, then you must do the same thing again.
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	if you are able to reach it and remove all the corruption, then restore the limb.
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is thus healthy, that is good.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, it means that the corruption is too far gone, that you cannot proceed;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other method than to wait for nature.
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there is a small bone corrupted, and you can remove it with pincers, if it is not removed by the proper instrument, and if there are many bones, then remove them all, do not leave any behind.
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	And if the moisture makes it contrary, and there is no mistake or fear, then boil and burn the bones, and deliver them.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And if you cannot remove them within an hour, place on the wound something poisonous, and leave it until the flesh is rotten around the bones, and then they will more easily break.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	And if it is large bones, such as a leg or thigh, then separate them as much as possible from the corruption until the entire bone is rotten, then reopen the wound.
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is a large part of the corruption, and it comes out in a mass with the bone;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	then it should be covered all around with the corruption, and then treated until it is sound.
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	And I will tell you about a fistula that happened to a man in his leg, so that you may take example and help in your work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young man around 30 years old, who had pain in his leg due to a cause that came from within the body, so that the matter came to the leg, and was filled with a large abscess, and there was no reason to open it.
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	But the doctors over-opened it so much that the abscess was opened, and they drained a lot of matter, and became a fistula, and there was much pain that everyone was groaning from the body's moisture.
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	and many sought cure within two years, and there was no knowledge in the art of hands, until I was called, and saw her leg and the remedies used to treat it, and what flowed through the pustules with great force.
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	and became red the veins of youth, and had the color yellow.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus, et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	I pitched a tent in one of these holes, and then I searched all the holes, and found that one was coming into contact with the other from all parts of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os, et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	I therefore hastened, and cut into one of the pustules until I discovered a part of the bone, and found it rotten and pierced, and the corruption was coming from within the bone.
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	I thought what appeared to me from the rotten bone, and I thought there was no other corruption, except that which I had seen.
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	and began to heal the wound with medicinal powders by long stitches, and could not hold.
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	then began again, and discovered the bone as before, and found continuous corruption in the bone, and the marrow, and then removed it, and I could not heal the limb.
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	but I could only place around one palm of the bone, and treat it to all its length, then heal it with medicines.
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	and it became healed and healed quickly, but did not want to begin the work again except for the weakness of the pain, which could not bear, and for the fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	For the evacuation of blood often caused harm, but he was completely healed, and in the place of the bone grew a hard callus, and it was of good disposition and had no harm or contradiction throughout, neither to the other nor to the coming.
