Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And the resetting, when it is possible to reset it, is that you extend your hand to both of yours.
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And its arms are spread, and the hands on both sides of the shoulder, in and out, and push the joint towards its pits, or to the root of its palm, until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is in front, it returns when he doubles his hand to his hand, and holds the root of the palm which is misaligned.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not return to its place, then administer strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	and it is that two ministers extend the arm, and they tie it with two ministers, so that it does not move during extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	then turn the arm from every part, then that you have wrapped a double long and wide cloth;
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	and when the patient sees the joint at their hand, if there is any oil to soften the joint, then rub the joint gently until it returns;
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, put above the dry plaster with some wool, and let it rest, and put the arm on the back of the bad, and leave it for some time, then remove it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	And if the joint is firmly in its place, let it rest;
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	and if you see that the joint is not healing well, restart the bandage and the limb, and let it rest thus for some time, until it is firmly placed;
puis le deslie.	then let it rest.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	and if it feels gritty after the resetting of the joint, and it moves, then bathe and rub it well, and press until it is relieved;
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	or you put a thick woolen grease on the joint, then let it rest for a day and a night, then remove it, and make it enter into a bath;
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	And when it moves, rub the joint immediately, then reset the bone, and then give a bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And thus do it twice or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	And if you see, then place warm moist flour with butter on top, and strain it.
si revenra a sa disposition.	It will return to its proper position.
li dislocation de la main	the dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The joint of the hand is loose, and the return is lighter than other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it should be returned to its place immediately, in the same manner as it is dislocated, provided that the muscles are inflamed or there is an abscess forming.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And when recalling, it is that you place your hand on the affected area, and extend the minister's hand, and the patient's hand is placed evenly, so that he places his palm on the appearance of the joint, and pushes until it returns.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	In any case, you must check if it is properly reset.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then place your hand on the back of his hand on the table for extension and recalling.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is in the back of the hand, put the patient's back of their hand on the table, and the other person puts their hand over the appearance of the joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns now, it is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If not, apply soothing counter-irritants and let it rest before starting again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you cannot put it back in place after some time, then the joint will remain twisted.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and will not heal without pain until the hand is washed, and nothing can be strained at all.
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	Therefore, if the nerve is cut or the artery:
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	then there is no other remedy but to cauterize the wound with fire, and perhaps nothing else will help.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, put the plaster we have mentioned above it, then tighten and leave it for five days, then remove and leave it like this.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it cannot be moved well, and there is no pain, then apply hot water and rub it until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	of the dislocation of the two fingers
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Never dislocate both fingers at once, never at the back of the palm or on the wrist.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	then the two shoulders, and push the dislocation with your hands until it returns, then support the head of the shoulder, and push it towards the part where it is disjointed.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	and let it rest for two days, and then put it back in place.
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	and bind it with a bandage as we have said, and the dislocation of the day, and the movement, and the binding.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this often, until it is straight, and everything else do the same, if it is dislocated in the belly of the hand, and do as you have done before, until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	and do the same when it is dislocated on the other side.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	back pain from the curvature of the spine
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the curvature of the spine or neck is dislocated, and there are many dislocations, there is no cure, for the patient dies from the pain.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are such that the dislocation suddenly moves out of place, and it cannot be held, and often soften any limb, or both elbows or the two arms or one.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the shoulder moves at an angle of four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	which is called "glenohumeral" if it moves to the back.
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The cure is that you reward the glenohumeral if it has come from childhood.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	if there is no cure or healing until now.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And those that come from falling or from blows or similar things, they said the old ways of healing with great words, which did not help much at all.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	but I have abbreviated it according to my intention, and have made instruments in various ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the globules which come before the worst, there is no remedy or health.
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	and also those that come directly in the second rib, and one cannot cure except for that proper one which comes to the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	and it is that the pain should be extended over his face in one even line, and he should have some strain away from him, so he does not bleed.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	then apply the following bandages to the head in earth-colored cloth, and the other on the feet, and tie a bandage around the leg without the painful area, and the other on the back, and hips, and knees, and ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and two ministers tie the bandages, one on the head and the other on the feet, among the two bandages.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and they should be well tied, the bandage as we have said, and the minister places his palms on the spine, until it returns.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return by this treatment, take a traction table of three arms long, and turn the painful area away from it, and the painful areas should be on the side, and press the head of the table away from the painful area, then place the middle of the table on the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and place the patient's feet on the other shoulder of the table, and press well until it returns to its place.
et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	and if you see, do it to the thumb that turns to the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And it is that you fix two ropes at the head of the dislocated arm of a strong person, and on each side of the feet, and between each rope, outside and inside, a long span of distance.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	and let there be in each rope one knot, where the thumb is straight, and the ropes are firmly on the ground, so that they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	and between each two ropes, let there be one rope turning, around which the thumb turns, and in the two turnings, two small ropes of a long span, to turn the thumb.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	Then tie the ligament that is among the tendons at the top of the shoulder, and the other ligament towards the feet at the other end, and each of the ministers turns its end to all the ligament, and the masters put the spine evenly as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, put a drying plaster with abundant sulfur on top, then the dressings, and then the splint of a tablet of three fingers in length, which preserves the shoulder from the disease and the part of the spine healthy, then tie it with a ligament, as we have said, and use the subtle bandages until they are healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if no remedy comes at the end of the illness, then one must administer medicines that are soothing and stimulating, with the advice we have given before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and never administer a piece of lead, and never appear in the back of the spine, and be careful that it is not a dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and it is the bones that are open, for which we should not have any presumption:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	by chance it would bring death.
des dislocations de la hainche	of shoulder dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	It should be noted that the joints of the waist and the joints of the shoulder come only from dislocations alone, and not like other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the hip joint is dislocated in four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	forward and backward;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more inwardly than that, and slightly dislocated forward and backward.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocation inward is such that when the misaligned leg is joined with the healthy one, it is longer and more open than the healthy ones, and the misaligned cannot double over at the fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and it is the thighs that are inflamed with abscesses, for the reason that the patient has lain there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of those who come after is that this accident is contrary to what has been mentioned before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of those who have it in front are that they keep their leg well aligned according to the completion;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	Throughout, do not double the angle of the joint with pain, and if they wish to move it, if they cannot, and retain their urine, and swell the wound, and when they go, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of those who come after are that they cannot spread their knee, nor double over, and that leg is more twisted than the other, and the anger is softened, and they have a pain in the ribs on the side.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The removal of this similar dislocation is that you reset it if it is old, and it stays according to its nature, without any treatment.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	And there is no need for it to have pride.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in this case where the dislocation is fresh, and it is of four kinds of dislocation, you must hurry to return the joint, and extend it inward and outward, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	If by chance it returns, and there is no other treatment needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return in this manner, then you must apply forceful treatment, and extend the leg firmly at two fingers, or at one joint that is connected to the thigh.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	And other treatments extend their hand above in this manner that they push their hands away from their armpits, then squeeze a cloth connected to the belly.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And other treatments grip the head of the joint.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	And they extend above and below at once, until the pain is raised from the ground once and remains hanging.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for four similar cases, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is well.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then you must put care to its appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder, you must first support the misaligned arm on its sound side, then place the bone over the root of the shoulder blade, and the limb that is outside the arm, then extend the bone upwards towards the arm and the collarbone;
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	then take other assistants to hold his arms, and grasp the large bone of the misaligned shoulder blade, and extend it behind him in a proper manner;
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	if it returns to its place now.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is less painful than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot hold it in this manner that we have said, then it is necessary to bind the two affected feet together with a strong silk rope above the two heels, and above the two ankles, and let the affected leg be extended two fingers more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then it should be hung from the head of a stick, and suspended above the ground two arms' length.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then command the surgeon to grasp the neck of the wound, and have other surgeons hang with the affected leg, who grasp the wound properly, as the joint is now healing quickly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	When the dislocation is in the shoulder, if the hairs are pricked as we mentioned in the case of gout, and the joint is held steady above the misaligned leg properly, and also above the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then apply two bandages, one at the top and the other at the foot, then fold the bandage between the thighs over the misaligned area.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And place wet cloths around, so it does not become dry, then stretch each helper towards him, and the mirror put equal to his hand, the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on the flat surface, and press as we have described in the grease, and cut the hairs off the sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to stretch the misaligned leg quickly, as I have said.
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and places the fingers' pain above the bad joint, then presses with the other hand, and stretches it down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is on the other side, it does not require extending the bad joint downwards, nor lifting up towards the earth, but it should be as it was when it was dislocated on the other side, as we have said of the position of the two shoulders;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and it should be on its face, and the arm extended as we have said before, and one must press on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be in place when the bad joint extends its legs, and they will be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Then apply heat to the knees, and put on the ointment, and wrap it in a bandage, so that it does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	And rests for three or four days, then reset it, and put on the ointment.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are even, tighten the bandage as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then reset it, and make the limb move well, until the member is comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	of the shoulder dislocation
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, from the inside and outside, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not dislocate again before.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you command the patient to bend their leg at the knee, and if they cannot straighten it at the knee, then they are dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit straight, extend their leg if they can, and put your back against their face, and put their foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take their knee to your palms, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee correctly.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And other ministers extend their foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that they can straighten their leg lightly at the knee.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and apply the plaster on it, and let the leg cool down at the thigh, and leave them together for three hours or four, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not work the hairs too much until the limb is comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limbs are not in place, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the back, until they are healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocated ankle
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The ankles are never bruised and never fully dislocated, neither inside nor outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And if the signs are that the joint is dislocated, and test before to the part where it is displaced:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	the return is light, and one should gently extend it to his hands when it is only slightly sore.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is displaced too soon, then you should make the hairs straight, and hold it with one hand at the leg, above the knee;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then draw the knife towards yourself with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, then extend it upwards, and strike the knife forcefully against the top.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, by striking and drawing the knife.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it returns, it is good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, if you start the work again, it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot return in this way, then lay the limb on its back on the ground, and insert a firm splint between its ribs, and wrap bandages around it, so that it does not bend the limb.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then the minister applies the poultice to the back, and other ministers extend the bandage over his hands or arms, so that it covers his neck.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each minister stretches evenly, and the bandages are placed between the fingers to hold the fingers in place as they stretch.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then the minister places the injured hand evenly on the dislocated joint, and other ministers apply a poultice to the healthy leg at the same time, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it has reached its point, if the plaster is applied and poultice is placed over it, and the bandage forms, and the bandage is tied to the leg, and the tendons that are above the ankle behind are warded off, so that the joints are not too stretched.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	then leave it for two days or three, and if its joints are not strong enough, then strain it.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	then reset it on the third day or fourth, and let it heal for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if it moves before that time, then it is certain that it will dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes, it is necessary to treat it as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed.
des dois	for two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, if they should be extended evenly with work, it is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any part of the body, then it is necessary to sit the patient on a flat surface or table, and place your hand over the joints, then press firmly until it returns.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even and there is no opening, then place the back of your hand on a flat surface, strain it firmly, leave it for three days, then reset it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let him rest until he is well.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wounds and of dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with the dislocation, and one wants to restore it, often times the patient dies from the pain:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not presumptuous in the cure, and if you are not wise in the art and have not used it long, and if you are not merciful and slow to act, then do not be harsh:
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of things, apply healing remedies gently, and leave the wound in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery:
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then reset the member at once as soon as the healing remedies come:
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	When the member is reset, administer things that soothe abscesses and cleanse the wound, as it should be, with dry applications of ointments.
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if the member breaks due to dislocation, and bones are broken, remove them, and do what we have said in simple diseases.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And beware of entering into the path of fear, as I have said, for it is better for you according to your Creator, and because of the knowledge of your arm and your body.
